# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Overview

**Task ID**: c_api_graphql_expert_079_architectural_understanding_expert_01

## Task Title

Architectural Migration Plan: Custom IPC to gRPC

## Description

The SynestheticCanvas API Suite is a high-performance, C-based microservices system. It currently uses a proprietary, low-level Inter-Process Communication (IPC) library, `sc_ipc`, for communication between the API Gateway and the backend microservices (`palette`, `texture`, `audio`, `narrative`). While this custom solution was performant for the initial design, it has become a maintenance burden and hinders plans to introduce new services written in other languages. The engineering leadership is evaluating a migration to gRPC for its standardized interface definition, cross-language support, and robust ecosystem. This task requires a deep architectural analysis of the existing system to produce a high-level migration plan.

## Your Task

You are a principal engineer tasked with evaluating the feasibility of migrating the SynestheticCanvas suite from its custom IPC mechanism to gRPC. Your analysis must be based on the provided file system.

Your deliverable is a technical report that addresses the following points:

1.  **Component Identification:** Identify and list all the specific files and modules across the entire codebase that constitute the current inter-service communication system. This includes the client-side implementation in the API Gateway, the server-side implementation in the microservices, and the shared library itself.

2.  **Data Flow Analysis:** Based on the code and documentation (especially `docs/architecture/data_flow.puml`), describe the end-to-end flow of a request from the API Gateway to a backend microservice (e.g., `texture-service`) and back. Detail the key functions, data structures, and libraries involved in this communication path.

3.  **Migration Strategy Proposal:** Outline a high-level, phased plan to migrate the `texture-service` and the API Gateway's communication with it to gRPC. Your plan must address:
    *   The necessary code and build system modifications (e.g., `CMakeLists.txt`) for both the API Gateway and the `texture-service`.
    *   A strategy for managing the transition to minimize or eliminate service downtime. How can the system operate with a mix of old and new IPC mechanisms simultaneously?
    *   A description of what the new gRPC-based communication flow would look like.

4.  **Risk Assessment:** Identify and explain the top 3-5 technical risks and challenges associated with this migration. Consider factors beyond just code changes, such as build complexity, performance characteristics, deployment, and operational management.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this task by systematically dissecting the architecture from multiple angles:

1.  **Top-Down Analysis:** Start with the documentation, specifically `docs/architecture/overview.md`, `docs/architecture/microservices.md`, and `docs/architecture/data_flow.puml`, to build a mental model of the system's components and their interactions.

2.  **Code-Level Investigation:**
    *   Identify the core IPC library, which is clearly `libs/sc_ipc/`. Analyze `sc_ipc.c` and its header to understand its API (e.g., functions for connecting, sending, receiving).
    *   Locate the client-side usage. A search for `sc_ipc` functions would lead to `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c`. This file is the linchpin for how the gateway communicates with all backend services.
    *   Locate the server-side usage. The `main.c` file for each microservice (e.g., `services/texture-service/src/main.c`) is the most likely place to find the server-side IPC initialization and request-handling loop.

3.  **Synthesize and Plan:**
    *   Trace a full request path: A GraphQL request hits a resolver in `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c`, which calls a function that uses the `service_client.c` to send a request via `sc_ipc`. The `texture-service`'s `main.c` receives this, passes it to `texture_handler.c`, which uses `texture_service.c` for business logic.
    *   For the migration plan, the expert would propose defining a `texture.proto` file for the gRPC service contract.
    *   They would suggest modifying the `CMakeLists.txt` for the gateway and the texture service to find and link the gRPC and Protobuf libraries.
    *   The core of the plan would involve a parallel deployment strategy. The `texture-service` would be modified to listen on two ports simultaneously: one for the old `sc_ipc` and one for the new `gRPC` server. The API Gateway's configuration (`sc_config`) would be extended to include a feature flag or a new service address, allowing it to select which protocol to use for the `texture-service`. This enables a gradual rollout without a "big bang" cutover.

4.  **Risk Identification:** The expert would think beyond the code and identify systemic risks: the complexity of adding gRPC's C++ dependencies to a C project's CMake build system, potential performance differences between a lean custom TCP protocol and HTTP/2-based gRPC, and the operational complexity of managing a hybrid-communication system during the transition period.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Component Identification Accuracy:** Did the agent correctly identify the key files (`service_client.c`, service `main.c` files, `sc_ipc.c`) responsible for the current IPC mechanism?
- **Architectural Flow Comprehension:** Was the agent able to accurately describe the request flow from the gateway to a microservice, referencing the correct modules (resolvers, service client, handlers)?
- **Migration Plan Viability:** Is the proposed migration plan technically sound and realistic? Does it include a phased rollout strategy (e.g., parallel systems) rather than a risky "big bang" approach?
- **Build & Dependency Awareness:** Did the agent recognize that modifying the `CMakeLists.txt` files and managing the gRPC/Protobuf dependencies is a non-trivial part of the task?
- **Risk Assessment Depth:** Did the agent identify sophisticated risks beyond simple coding errors, such as build system complexity, performance implications, and operational overhead during the transition?
- **Use of Evidence:** Does the agent's analysis refer to specific files, documentation (`data_flow.puml`), and architectural patterns to support its conclusions?

     1→/*
     2→ * sc_ipc.h
     3→ * ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
     4→ * SynestheticCanvas Inter-Process Communication (IPC) library – Public API
     5→ *
     6→ * The IPC layer allows individual SynestheticCanvas micro-services to exchange
     7→ * strongly-typed messages with predictable latency guarantees.  The transport
     8→ * is based on UNIX domain sockets with configurable timeouts, automatic
     9→ * envelope framing, and correlation identifiers for request/response
    10→ * matching.  The ABI is stable and versioned; breaking changes will bump
    11→ * SC_IPC_VERSION_MAJOR.
    12→ *
    13→ * Copyright (c) 2024
    14→ *   SynestheticCanvas Contributors <oss@synestheticcanvas.io>

    37→#   include <sys/un.h>
    38→#endif

    41→extern "C" {

     1→```markdown
     2→# SynestheticCanvas API Gateway (`api_graphql`)
     3→
     4→> “Every endpoint is a brush stroke.”  
     5→> The **SynestheticCanvas API Gateway** unifies a constellation of micro-services—palette management, dynamic texture synthesis, audio-reactive animation, and narrative branching—behind a single color-coded GraphQL & REST façade.  
     6→> Written in modern, production-grade **C17**, the gateway focuses on _performance_, _observability_, and _extensibility_.
     7→
     8→---
     9→
    10→## 1. Quick Start
    11→
    12→```bash
    13→# Clone & build the full constellation
    14→git clone --recurse-submodules https://github.com/synestheticlabs/synesthetic-canvas.git
    15→cd synesthetic-canvas/SynestheticCanvas/api-gateway
    16→mkdir build && cd build
    17→cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..
    18→make -j$(nproc)
    19→
    20→# Run gateway with default in-container config
    21→./sc-api-gateway --config ../config/gateway.toml
    22→```
    23→
    24→The gateway listens by default on:
    25→
    26→| Protocol | Port | Purpose                   |
    27→|----------|------|---------------------------|
    28→| HTTP/1.1 | 8080 | REST fallback endpoints   |
    29→| HTTP/2   | 8443 | GraphQL over TLS (gRPC)   |
    30→| UDP      | 8125 | Metrics (StatsD/Datadog)  |
    31→
    32→---
    33→
    34→## 2. Minimal Client Example (C17)
    35→
    36→Below is a self-contained example that queries the `currentPalette` GraphQL endpoint with pagination & version headers.  
    37→Build with: `cc -Wall -Wextra -pedantic -std=c17 client.c -lcurl -o client`
    38→

    40→/**

    45→ *  - GraphQL

I have completed the comprehensive technical report for the migration from custom IPC to gRPC. The solution has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md`.

## Summary of the Technical Report

The report addresses all four required deliverables:

### 1. Component Identification
I identified all files constituting the current inter-service communication system:
- **IPC Library**: `libs/sc_ipc/include/sc_ipc.h` and `libs/sc_ipc/src/sc_ipc.c` - UNIX domain socket-based IPC with length-prefixed framing
- **Gateway Client**: `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` - HTTP/REST client using libcurl
- **Service Servers**: Each microservice's `main.c` files (e.g., `services/texture-service/src/main.c`) using libmicrohttpd
- **Supporting files**: GraphQL resolvers, handlers, and CMakeLists.txt build files

### 2. Data Flow Analysis
I traced the end-to-end request flow based on `docs/architecture/data_flow.puml`:
1. Client → API Gateway (rate limiting, validation)
2. Gateway → GraphQL Resolver → Service Client (libcurl HTTP)
3. Service Client → Texture Service (libmicrohttpd)
4. Texture Service → Handler → Repository → Response

### 3. Migration Strategy
I proposed a 5-phase migration plan:
- **Phase 1**: Infrastructure setup (Protocol Buffer definitions, CMakeLists.txt modifications)
- **Phase 2**: Texture Service dual-protocol support (gRPC + HTTP simultaneously)
- **Phase 3**: API Gateway gRPC client with feature flag
- **Phase 4**: Gradual traffic migration (canary → full rollout)
- **Phase 5**: Legacy HTTP deprecation

Key strategy: **Parallel deployment** with feature flags allows zero-downtime migration and easy rollback.

### 4. Risk Assessment
I identified 5 technical risks:
1. **Build System Complexity (HIGH)**: gRPC C requires C++ dependencies
2. **Performance Regres

Vision\n\nSynestheticCanvas transforms every HTTP or WebSocket request into a _brush-stroke_ on a living digital canvas.  \nMicroservices supply the colors, textures, and motion, while the **GraphQL/REST gateway** orchestrates them into a single, time-synchronous response.  \nThe architecture has three non-negotiable goals:\n\n1. **Expressiveness** \u2013 Artists can combine services like mixing paint.  \n2. **Evolution** \u2013 New art forms (e.g., volumetric audio) can be added without breaking existing exhibitions.  \n3. **Performance** \u2013 Frame-accurate (< 16 ms) responses even under festival-scale load.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Macro-Level Topology\n\n```mermaid\nflowchart LR\n    subgraph Client Edge\n        VR[VR Headset]\n        Web[Web Frontend]\n        Bot[AI Bot]\n    end\n\n    subgraph Gateway Layer\n        GQL(GraphQL Gateway)\n        REST(REST Fallback)\n    end\n\n    subgraph Core Services\n        Palette(Palette Svc)\n        Synth(Texture Synth)\n        Audio(Audio-React)\n        Narr(Narrative Engine)\n    end\n    \n    subgraph Shared Infra\n        LogStack(ELK/OTel)\n        Redis((Redis Cache))\n        MQ((NATS JetStream))\n        PG[(PostgreSQL Cluster)]\n    end\n\n    VR -->|Query / Mutation| GQL\n    Web --> GQL\n    Bot --> REST\n    \n    GQL -- gRPC/json --> Palette & Synth & Audio & Narr\n    REST -- HTTP--> Palette & Synth & Audio & Narr\n    \n    GQL -- sub/ms logs --> LogStack\n    REST -- prometheus --> LogStack\n    \n    Palette --- PG\n    Synth --- Redis\n    Audio --- MQ\n    Narr  --- PG\n\n    classDef red fill:#ffdfe0,stroke:#ce2b37,stroke-width:2;\n    class REST red\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Layered Breakdown\n\n| Layer                | Responsibility                                           | Key Patterns                        |\n|----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------|\n| **Gateway**          | Auth, rate-limit, schema stitching, cache-aside          | API Gateway, GraphQL Schema         |\n| **Service Layer**    | Domain orchestrations, streaming, CQRS                   | Command/Query Separation            |\n| **Repository Layer** | Data access, DAO mapping, migrations                     | Repository Pattern                  |\n| **Infra**            | Observability, tracing, message bus, persistence         | Sidecar + 12-Factor                 |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Gateway Internals\n\n### 4.1 GraphQL Route Lifecycle\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant C as Client\n    participant G as Gateway\n    participant V as Validator\n    participant S as Service\n    participant L as Logger\n    \n    C->>G: gql { mutateTexture(...) }\n    G->>V: schema.validate(request)\n    V->>G: Ok / Err\n    alt Err\n        G->>C: 422 Unprocessable Entity\n        G->>L: warn(validation)\n    else Ok\n        G->>S: gRPC call (texture-synth)\n        S-->>G: TexturePayload\n        G->>L: info(request)\n        G->>C: 200 + JSON\n    end\n```\n\n#### 4.1.1 Validation Rules\n* **Static** \u2013 schema-compiled (enum ranges, non-null fields)  \n* **Dynamic** \u2013 cross-service (`audioId` exists, `paletteId` owns user)  \n* **Security** \u2013 depth limit, cost analysis, JWT claims scoping  \n\n### 4.2 REST Fallback\n\n* Code-generated from the GraphQL schema using `gnostic` + custom templates.  \n* Follows HATEOAS, supports `?page[limit]=`, `?page[offset]=` for pagination.  \n\n---\n\n## 5. Versioning Strategy\n\n1. Breaking changes \u2192 new _major_ (e.g., `v2`) schema namespace.  \n2. Additive changes \u2192 patch bump (`v1.3 \u2192 v1.4`) and feature flag.  \n3. Deprecated fields emit `Deprecation-Notice` headers for 90 days.  \n\n```\nquery v1_3 {\n  palette(id: \"ultra-violet\") {          # valid\n    swatches { hex }                     \n  }\n}\n\nquery v2_0 {\n  paletteGet(id: \"ultra-violet\") {       # renamed\n    swatches { hex, rgb }                # new field\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Service Blueprint (C Reference)\n\nA microservice is a standalone **statically-linked** ELF built with **C17** and a thin **gRPC** layer.  \nBelow is a simplified excerpt from `palette_svc/src/service.c`.\n\n```c\n/**\n * @file service.c\n * @brief Palette microservice \u2013 Service entry point & request handlers.\n */\n\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n#include \"core/palette.h\"\n#include \"infra/logger.h\"\n#include \"infra/repository.h\"\n#include \"gen/palette.grpc.pb-c.h\"\n\nstatic palette_repo_t *repo = NULL;\n\n/* gRPC \u2192 C callback ------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic void handle_palette_get(\n        const PaletteGetRequest *req,\n        PaletteGetReply **resp,\n        void *user_data)\n{\n    (void)user_data;\n    sc_trace_span_t span = sc_trace_start(\"palette_get\");\n\n    /* 1. Validate -------------------------------- */\n    if (!req->id || req->id[0] == '\\0') {\n        sc_log_warn(\"palette_get: empty id\");\n        *resp = palette_get_reply__error(\n            HTTP_BAD_REQUEST, \"Palette ID must not be empty\");\n        goto finish;\n    }\n\n    /* 2. Repository ------------------------------ */\n    palette_t pal = {0};\n    sc_error_t err = repo->get(repo, req->id, &pal);\n    if (err.code == SC_ERR_NOT_FOUND) {\n        *resp = palette_get_reply__error(\n            HTTP_NOT_FOUND, \"Palette not found\");\n        goto finish;\n    } else if (err.code != SC_OK) {\n        sc_log_error(\"repo->get failed: %s\", err.msg);\n        *resp = palette_get_reply__error(\n            HTTP_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, \"Internal error\");\n        goto finish;\n    }\n\n    /* 3. Mapping \u2192 ProtoBuf ---------------------- */\n    *resp = palette_get_reply__success(&pal);\n\nfinish:\n    sc_trace_end(&span);\n}\n\nint main(int argc, char **argv)\n{\n    sc_logger_init_default();          /* JSON-structured logs          */\n    sc_trace_init_otel();              /* OpenTelemetry exporter        */\n\n    repo = palette_repo_init(getenv(\"PG_DSN\"));\n    if (!repo) {\n        sc_log_fatal(\"failed to init repository\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    sc_grpc_server_t *srv = sc_grpc_server_create(\"0.0.0.0:7001\");\n    sc_grpc_server_register_palette_get(srv, handle_palette_get, NULL);\n\n    /* Graceful shutdown ------------------------- */\n    signal(SIGTERM, sc_grpc_server_stop);\n    signal(SIGINT,  sc_grpc_server_stop);\n\n    sc_log_info(\"palette_svc listening on :7001\");\n    sc_grpc_server_serve(srv);\n\n    palette_repo_free(repo);\n    sc_grpc_server_free(srv);\n    sc_logger_flush();\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Observability & Monitoring\n\n| Metric                    | Target             | Alert Threshold                    |\n|---------------------------|--------------------|------------------------------------|\n| `http_request_duration`   | < 150 ms p95       | > 250 ms for 5 min                 |\n| `grpc_error_rate`         | < 0.2 %            | > 5 % rolling 1 min                |\n| `redis_cache_hit_ratio`   | > 0.9              | < 0.7 rolling 15 min               |\n| `jetstream_lag`           | < 1 msg           | > 50 msg for 30 s                  |\n\nLogs are shipped to **ELK**, traces to **Jaeger**, metrics scraped by **Prometheus** and rendered in **Grafana** dashboards (`dashboards/` folder).\n\n---\n\n## 8. Security Posture\n\n* **mTLS** between services (`SPIFFE` identities).  \n* **OPA** sidecar on gateway for fine-grained policy.  \n* Every JWT carries:\n  - `cid` (canvas-id) \u2013 tenant sharding\n  - `scopes` \u2013 `palette:rw`, `texture:r`  \n  - `aud` (service audience)  \n\n*Rate limiting* \u2013 token-bucket (Redis) keyed by `sub:cid`.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Failure Modes & Resilience\n\n| Scenario                        | Mitigation                                  |\n|---------------------------------|---------------------------------------------|\n| Network partition               | gRPC retries + circuit-breaker (Hystrix-c)  |\n| Gateway overload                | Adaptive LRU cache, request shedder         |\n| Service crash                   | Kubernetes restart, health probes           |\n| DB connection pool exhaustion   | PgBouncer & slow-query logger               |\n| Upstream incompatible version   | Dual-run old/new schema + feature flags     |\n\n---\n\n## 10. Deployment Pipeline\n\n1. **Pre-merge** \u2013 `clang-tidy`, `cppcheck`, `unit-tests` (CTEST).  \n2. **Build** \u2013 `docker build --platform=linux/amd64 --target runtime`.  \n3. **Security** \u2013 `trivy fs`, SBOM via `syft`.  \n4. **Canary** \u2013 5 % traffic for 30 min, monitored saturation SLOs.  \n5. **Promotion** \u2013 Git tag + Helm release (`charts/`).  \n\n---\n\n## 11. Glossary\n\n| Term       | Meaning                                                    |\n|------------|------------------------------------------------------------|\n| Brush-Stroke | Individual API call altering the live canvas state.       |\n| Swatch       | A semantically-named color token (`#FF22AA`, \u201cultra-violet\u201d). |\n| Texture Node | Procedural fragment generating a 2D/3D texture.          |\n| Narrative Arc| Branch in story graph triggered by user input.           |\n\n---\n\n## 12. References\n\n* _Reactive Design Patterns_ \u2013 R. Kuhn  \n* _Clean Architecture in C_ \u2013 A. Martin  \n* GraphQL Spec `2021-10`  \n* OpenTelemetry v1.26.0  \n\n---\n\n> \u00a9 2024 SynestheticCanvas Consortium \u2013 Released under the Apache 2.0 License\n```",

\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\nEach micro-service encapsulates exactly one creative concern and  \ncommunicates through HTTP/2 + Protocol Buffers over gRPC *internally*  \nand GraphQL/REST *externally*.\n\n---\n\n## 2  Common Library: `sc_core`\n\nAll services link against a minimal abstraction library that standardises\nlogging, config, tracing, JSON and Protobuf helpers.\n\n```c\n/* File: sc_core/logger.h */\n#ifndef SC_CORE_LOGGER_H\n#define SC_CORE_LOGGER_H\n\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <time.h>\n\ntypedef enum {\n    SC_LOG_DEBUG,\n    SC_LOG_INFO,\n    SC_LOG_WARN,\n    SC_LOG_ERROR\n} sc_log_level_t;\n\n/**\n * Initialise the global logger.\n * @param level Minimum level that will be emitted.\n * @return 0 on success, -1 on failure (errno is set).\n */\nint sc_log_init(sc_log_level_t level);\n\n/**\n * Log a formatted message. Always thread-safe.\n */\nvoid sc_log(sc_log_level_t level, const char *fmt, ...);\n\n/* Convenience macros */\n#define SC_LOGD(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_DEBUG, __VA_ARGS__)\n#define SC_LOGI(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_INFO,  __VA_ARGS__)\n#define SC_LOGW(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_WARN,  __VA_ARGS__)\n#define SC_LOGE(...) sc_log(SC_LOG_ERROR, __VA_ARGS__)\n\n#endif /* SC_CORE_LOGGER_H */\n```\n\n```c\n/* File: sc_core/logger.c */\n#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L\n#include \"logger.h\"\n#include <stdarg.h>\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\nstatic struct {\n    sc_log_level_t min_level;\n    pthread_mutex_t mtx;\n    FILE *stream;\n} g_ctx = { .min_level = SC_LOG_INFO, .mtx = PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER,\n            .stream = NULL };\n\nstatic const char *level_to_str(sc_log_level_t lvl) {\n    switch (lvl) {\n        case SC_LOG_DEBUG: return \"DEBUG\";\n        case SC_LOG_INFO:  return \"INFO \";\n        case SC_LOG_WARN:  return \"WARN \";\n        default:           return \"ERROR\";\n    }\n}\n\nint sc_log_init(sc_log_level_t level) {\n    g_ctx.min_level = level;\n    g_ctx.stream = stderr;\n    return 0;\n}\n\nvoid sc_log(sc_log_level_t level, const char *fmt, ...) {\n    if (level < g_ctx.min_level) return;\n\n    time_t now = time(NULL);\n    struct tm tm_now;\n    localtime_r(&now, &tm_now);\n\n    char ts[32];\n    strftime(ts, sizeof ts, \"%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S\", &tm_now);\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&g_ctx.mtx);\n    fprintf(g_ctx.stream, \"%s [%s] \", ts, level_to_str(level));\n\n    va_list ap;\n    va_start(ap, fmt);\n    vfprintf(g_ctx.stream, fmt, ap);\n    va_end(ap);\n\n    fputc('\\n', g_ctx.stream);\n    fflush(g_ctx.stream);\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&g_ctx.mtx);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3  Canonical Service Template\n\nEvery new service clones this template, wires its domain logic, and registers\nwith Consul for discovery.\n\n```c\n/* File: svc_template/main.c */\n#define _DEFAULT_SOURCE\n#include <microhttpd.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include \"router.h\"\n\n#define PORT 8080\n\nstatic volatile sig_atomic_t running = 1;\n\nstatic void handle_sig(int sig) {\n    (void)sig;\n    running = 0;\n}\n\nint main(void) {\n    /* 1. Initialise cross-cutting concerns */\n    sc_log_init(SC_LOG_DEBUG);\n\n    SC_LOGI(\"Starting Palette Service v1.2.0\");\n\n    /* 2. Configure graceful termination */\n    struct sigaction sa = { .sa_handler = handle_sig };\n    sigaction(SIGINT, &sa, NULL);\n    sigaction(SIGTERM, &sa, NULL);\n\n    /* 3. Start HTTP daemon */\n    struct MHD_Daemon *daemon = MHD_start_daemon(\n        MHD_USE_SELECT_INTERNALLY | MHD_USE_EPOLL_INTERNALLY,\n        PORT, NULL, NULL, &router_dispatch, NULL,\n        MHD_OPTION_CONNECTION_TIMEOUT,  (unsigned int)10,\n        MHD_OPTION_END);\n\n    if (!daemon) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"Failed to start HTTP daemon\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    /* 4. Main loop */\n    while (running) {\n        sleep(1);\n    }\n\n    /* 5. Shutdown */\n    MHD_stop_daemon(daemon);\n    SC_LOGI(\"Shutdown complete\");\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```\n\n`router_dispatch` is generated by a compile-time code-gen step that turns an\nOpenAPI spec (`openapi.yaml`) and a GraphQL schema (`schema.graphql`) into a\nmultipart dispatcher.  \nFor brevity, we hand-write a minimal implementation below.\n\n---\n\n## 4  Case Study \u2013 Palette Management Service\n\n### 4.1  Domain Model\n\n```c\n/* File: palette/model.h */\n#ifndef PALETTE_MODEL_H\n#define PALETTE_MODEL_H\n\n#include <stdint.h>\n\ntypedef struct {\n    uint32_t id;\n    char     name[64];\n    uint8_t  r, g, b, a;\n} palette_t;\n\n#endif /* PALETTE_MODEL_H */\n```\n\n### 4.2  Repository Layer\n\n```c\n/* File: palette/repository.h */\n#ifndef PALETTE_REPOSITORY_H\n#define PALETTE_REPOSITORY_H\n\n#include \"model.h\"\n#include <stddef.h>\n\n/**\n * Create or update a palette. Returns 0 on success.\n */\nint palette_repo_save(const palette_t *p);\n\n/**\n * Retrieve a palette by ID.\n * @return 0 on success, -ENOENT if not found.\n */\nint palette_repo_get(uint32_t id, palette_t *out);\n\n/**\n * Paginated list of palettes.\n * @param offset Zero-based.\n * @param limit  Max items.\n * @param out    Pre-allocated buffer.\n * @return number of items written, or negative on error.\n */\nssize_t palette_repo_list(size_t offset, size_t limit, palette_t *out);\n\n#endif /* PALETTE_REPOSITORY_H */\n```\n\n```c\n/* File: palette/repository_sqlite.c */\n#define _GNU_SOURCE\n#include \"repository.h\"\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include <sqlite3.h>\n#include <errno.h>\n\nstatic sqlite3 *db = NULL;\n\nstatic int ensure_db(void) {\n    if (db) return 0;\n    int rc = sqlite3_open(\"data/palette.db\", &db);\n    if (rc != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite open error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    char *err = NULL;\n    const char *ddl =\n        \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS palette (\"\n        \"id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY,\"\n        \"name TEXT NOT NULL,\"\n        \"r INTEGER NOT NULL,\"\n        \"g INTEGER NOT NULL,\"\n        \"b INTEGER NOT NULL,\"\n        \"a INTEGER NOT NULL);\";\n    rc = sqlite3_exec(db, ddl, NULL, NULL, &err);\n    if (rc != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite DDL error: %s\", err);\n        sqlite3_free(err);\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    return 0;\n}\n\nint palette_repo_save(const palette_t *p) {\n    if (!p) return -EINVAL;\n    if (ensure_db() < 0) return -EIO;\n\n    const char *sql =\n        \"INSERT INTO palette(id, name, r, g, b, a) \"\n        \"VALUES(?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5, ?6) \"\n        \"ON CONFLICT(id) DO UPDATE SET \"\n        \"name=excluded.name, r=excluded.r, g=excluded.g, \"\n        \"b=excluded.b, a=excluded.a;\";\n\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite prepare error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 1, p->id);\n    sqlite3_bind_text  (stmt, 2, p->name, -1, SQLITE_TRANSIENT);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 3, p->r);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 4, p->g);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 5, p->b);\n    sqlite3_bind_int   (stmt, 6, p->a);\n\n    int rc = sqlite3_step(stmt);\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return (rc == SQLITE_DONE) ? 0 : -EIO;\n}\n\nint palette_repo_get(uint32_t id, palette_t *out) {\n    if (!out) return -EINVAL;\n    if (ensure_db() < 0) return -EIO;\n\n    const char *sql = \"SELECT id, name, r, g, b, a FROM palette WHERE id=?1;\";\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite prepare error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    sqlite3_bind_int(stmt, 1, id);\n\n    int rc = sqlite3_step(stmt);\n    if (rc == SQLITE_ROW) {\n        out->id   = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 0);\n        strncpy(out->name, (const char *)sqlite3_column_text(stmt, 1), sizeof out->name);\n        out->r    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 2);\n        out->g    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 3);\n        out->b    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 4);\n        out->a    = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 5);\n        sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n        return 0;\n    }\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return -ENOENT;\n}\n\nssize_t palette_repo_list(size_t offset, size_t limit, palette_t *out) {\n    if (!out || !limit) return -EINVAL;\n    if (ensure_db() < 0) return -EIO;\n\n    const char *sql =\n        \"SELECT id, name, r, g, b, a FROM palette \"\n        \"ORDER BY id LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2;\";\n    sqlite3_stmt *stmt = NULL;\n    if (sqlite3_prepare_v2(db, sql, -1, &stmt, NULL) != SQLITE_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"SQLite prepare error: %s\", sqlite3_errmsg(db));\n        return -EIO;\n    }\n    sqlite3_bind_int(stmt, 1, limit);\n    sqlite3_bind_int(stmt, 2, offset);\n\n    ssize_t count = 0;\n    while (sqlite3_step(stmt) == SQLITE_ROW && count < (ssize_t)limit) {\n        palette_t *p = &out[count++];\n        p->id = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 0);\n        strncpy(p->name, (const char *)sqlite3_column_text(stmt, 1), sizeof p->name);\n        p->r = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 2);\n        p->g = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 3);\n        p->b = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 4);\n        p->a = sqlite3_column_int(stmt, 5);\n    }\n    sqlite3_finalize(stmt);\n    return count;\n}\n```\n\n### 4.3  REST + GraphQL Router\n\n```c\n/* File: svc_template/router.c */\n#include <microhttpd.h>\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include \"palette/repository.h\"\n#include <cjson/cJSON.h>\n#include <string.h>\n\nstatic int json_response(struct MHD_Connection *conn,\n                         const cJSON *json, int status) {\n    char *payload = cJSON_PrintUnformatted(json);\n    struct MHD_Response *resp =\n        MHD_create_response_from_buffer(strlen(payload), payload,\n                                        MHD_RESPMEM_MUST_FREE);\n    if (!resp) return MHD_NO;\n\n    MHD_add_response_header(resp, \"Content-Type\", \"application/json\");\n    int ret = MHD_queue_response(conn, status, resp);\n    MHD_destroy_response(resp);\n    return ret;\n}\n\nstatic int handle_get_palette(struct MHD_Connection *conn,\n                              uint32_t id) {\n    palette_t p;\n    if (palette_repo_get(id, &p) != 0) {\n        cJSON *err = cJSON_CreateObject();\n        cJSON_AddStringToObject(err, \"error\", \"Palette not found\");\n        return json_response(conn, err, MHD_HTTP_NOT_FOUND);\n    }\n\n    cJSON *json = cJSON_CreateObject();\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"id\",   p.id);\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(json, \"name\", p.name);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"r\",    p.r);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"g\",    p.g);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"b\",    p.b);\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(json, \"a\",    p.a);\n    return json_response(conn, json, MHD_HTTP_OK);\n}\n\nint router_dispatch(void *cls,\n                    struct MHD_Connection *connection,\n                    const char *url, const char *method,\n                    const char *ver, const char *upload_data,\n                    size_t *upload_data_size, void **con_cls) {\n    (void)cls; (void)ver; (void)upload_data; (void)upload_data_size; (void)con_cls;\n\n    SC_LOGD(\"Incoming %s %s\", method, url);\n\n    /* Example route: GET /v1/palette/<id> */\n    if (strcmp(method, \"GET\") == 0 &&\n        strncmp(url, \"/v1/palette/\", 12) == 0) {\n\n        uint32_t id = (uint32_t)strtoul(url + 12, NULL, 10);\n        return handle_get_palette(connection, id);\n    }\n\n    /* Default 404 */\n    cJSON *err = cJSON_CreateObject();\n    cJSON_AddStringToObject(err, \"error\", \"Route not found\");\n    return json_response(connection, err, MHD_HTTP_NOT_FOUND);\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5  GraphQL Gateway Stub\n\nThe gateway composes service schemas using Apollo Federation syntax\nand delegates sub-queries through the internal gRPC mesh.  \nBelow is a trimmed skeleton that wraps our Palette service.\n\n```c\n/* File: gateway/resolvers/palette_resolver.c */\n#include \"sc_core/logger.h\"\n#include <grpc/grpc.h>\n#include <grpc/byte_buffer.h>\n#include \"generated/palette.grpc.pb-c.h\"\n\nbool gql_resolve_palette(struct gql_query_ctx *ctx) {\n    uint32_t id = gql_arg_u32(ctx, \"id\");\n    Palette__GetRequest req = PALETTE__GET_REQUEST__INIT;\n    req.id = id;\n\n    /* Send over gRPC */\n    grpc_channel *ch = grpc_insecure_channel_create(\"palette:50051\", NULL, NULL);\n    grpc_call *call = grpc_channel_create_call(\n        ch, NULL, GRPC_PROPAGATE_DEFAULT, ctx->cq,\n        grpc_slice_from_static_string(\"/palette.Palette/Get\"),\n        NULL, gpr_inf_future(GPR_CLOCK_REALTIME), NULL);\n\n    grpc_metadata_array md_arr;\n    grpc_metadata_array_init(&md_arr);\n\n    grpc_byte_buffer *payload =\n        grpc_raw_byte_buffer_create(NULL, 0);\n\n    grpc_op ops[6];\n    memset(ops, 0, sizeof ops);\n    ops[0].op = GRPC_OP_SEND_INITIAL_METADATA;\n    ops[0].data.send_initial_metadata.count = 0;\n\n    ops[1].op = GRPC_OP_SEND_MESSAGE;\n    ops[1].data.send_message.send_message = payload;\n\n    ops[2].op = GRPC_OP_SEND_CLOSE_FROM_CLIENT;\n\n    ops[3].op = GRPC_OP_RECV_INITIAL_METADATA;\n    ops[3].data.recv_initial_metadata.recv_initial_metadata = &md_arr;\n\n    grpc_status_code status;\n    grpc_slice details;\n    ops[4].op = GRPC_OP_RECV_STATUS_ON_CLIENT;\n    ops[4].data.recv_status_on_client.status = &status;\n    ops[4].data.recv_status_on_client.status_details = &details;\n\n    grpc_call_error cerr = grpc_call_start_batch(call, ops, 5, NULL, NULL);\n    if (cerr != GRPC_CALL_OK) {\n        SC_LOGE(\"gRPC start batch failed\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    grpc_completion_queue_pluck(ctx->cq, NULL, gpr_inf_future(GPR_CLOCK_REALTIME), NULL);\n\n    /* Transform Protobuf to GraphQL JSON */\n    if (status != GRPC_STATUS_OK) {\n        gql_error(ctx, \"Palette service error\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /* Omitted: decode response into ctx->response */\n\n    grpc_metadata_array_destroy(&md_arr);\n    grpc_byte_buffer_destroy(payload);\n    grpc_call_destroy(call);\n    grpc_channel_destroy(ch);\n    return true;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6  Versioning & Lifecycle\n\n- Every service exposes `/version` returning `{ \"semver\": \"x.y.z\", \"git\": \"<sha>\" }`.\n- GraphQL schemas are versioned via `@link(import:)` directives.\n- REST endpoints embed a major version in the URL (`/v1/`, `/v2/`).\n- Obsolete routes remain available for *one* minor version with deprecation\n  warnings in the response headers.\n\n---\n\n## 7  Observability & Resilience\n\n1. **Structured logging** (`JSON` when `LOG_FORMAT=json` env var is set).  \n2. **Metrics** exported via `/metrics` in Prometheus format.  \n3. **Tracing** instrumented through OpenTelemetry C SDK.  \n4. **Circuit-breaker** wrapper auto-generated around every gRPC stub.  \n5. **Rate-limiting** handled at the API Gateway using the Token-Bucket\n   algorithm (Redis backend).\n\n---\n\n## 8  Build & Deployment\n\n```\n$ mkdir build && cd build\n$ cmake -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release ..\n$ make -j$(nproc)\n$ docker build -t synesthetic/palette:1.2.0 services/palette\n$ helm upgrade --install palette charts/palette\n```\n\nCI jobs run `clang-tidy`, `cppcheck`, unit tests (cmocka), and integration\ntests spun up with `testcontainers-c`.\n\n---\n\n## 9  Appendix \u2013 Compile Flags\n\n```\n-std=c17\n-Wall -Wextra -Werror\n-pedantic\n-fno-common\n-fsanitize=address,undefined\n```\n\n```",

The transport\n * is based on UNIX domain sockets with configurable timeouts, automatic\n * envelope framing, and correlation identifiers for request/response\n * matching.  The ABI is stable and versioned; breaking changes will bump\n * SC_IPC_VERSION_MAJOR.\n *\n * Copyright (c) 2024\n *   SynestheticCanvas Contributors <oss@synestheticcanvas.io>\n *   Licensed under false;\n\n    if (pthread_rwlock_init(&state->lock, NULL) != 0)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INTERNAL, \"Failed to initialize rwlock: %s\", strerror(errno));\n        free(state);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    state->ready = true;\n    log_info(\"[texture-handler] Initialized successfully\");\n\n    return (TextureHandler *)state;\n}\n\nvoid texture_handler_dispose(TextureHandler *handler)\n{\n    if (!handler)\n        return;\n\n    TextureHandlerState *state = (TextureHandlerState *)handler;\n    pthread_rwlock_destroy(&state->lock);\n    /* Repository and metrics lifetime are managed by the caller */\n    free(state);\n}\n\n/**\n * Create a new texture based on the DTO provided by higher layers. This\n * function validates all fields, generates an ID, persists the record, and\n * returns a deep-copied Texture object that the caller must free.\n */\nTexture *texture_handler_create(TextureHandler *handler,\n                                const TextureInput *input,\n                                TextureError *err)\n{\n    TextureHandlerState *state = (TextureHandlerState *)handler;\n    if (!state || !state->ready)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_NOT_INITIALIZED, \"TextureHandler is not initialized\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    /* Validate input first */\n    if (!_validate_texture_input(input, err))\n        return NULL;\n\n    /* Build Texture domain object */\n    Texture tx      = {0};\n    tx.id           = _generate_uuid();\n    tx.name         = strndup(input->name, MAX_TEXTURE_NAME_LEN);\n    tx.color_profile= strndup(input->color_profile, MAX_COLOR_PROFILE_LEN);\n    tx.width        = input->width;\n    tx.height       = input->height;\n    tx.created_at   = (uint64_t)time(NULL);\n\n    if (!tx.id || !tx.name || !tx.color_profile)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_OOM, \"Failed to allocate texture attributes\");\n        goto cleanup_fail;\n    }\n\n    /* Serialize metadata payload */\n    tx.metadata = _texture_to_json(&tx, err);\n    if (!tx.metadata)\n        goto cleanup_fail;\n\n    /* Acquire write-lock for repository update */\n    if (pthread_rwlock_wrlock(&state->lock) != 0)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INTERNAL, \"Failed to acquire write lock\");\n        goto cleanup_fail;\n    }\n\n    bool persist_ok = repository_save_texture(state->repo, &tx, err);\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&state->lock);\n\n    if (!persist_ok)\n        goto cleanup_fail;\n\n    /* Metrics */\n    if (state->metrics)\n        metrics_counter_inc(state->metrics, \"texture_created_total\", 1);\n\n    /* Deep copy result for caller (repository may own original memory) */\n    Texture *result = texture_clone(&tx, err);\n    texture_free(&tx); /* Free local copy */\n\n    log_info(\"[texture-handler] Created texture '%s' (%ux%u)\", result->id, result->width, result->height);\n    return result;\n\ncleanup_fail:\n    texture_free(&tx);\n    return NULL;\n}\n\n/**\n * Retrieve a single texture by its UUID. Caller is responsible for freeing\n * the returned object via texture_free().\n */\nTexture *texture_handler_get(TextureHandler *handler, const char *texture_id, TextureError *err)\n{\n    TextureHandlerState *state = (TextureHandlerState *)handler;\n    if (!state || !state->ready)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_NOT_INITIALIZED, \"TextureHandler is not initialized\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (!validation_is_uuid(texture_id))\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INVALID_ARGUMENT, \"Invalid UUID provided: '%s'\", texture_id);\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (pthread_rwlock_rdlock(&state->lock) != 0)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INTERNAL, \"Failed to acquire read lock\");\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    Texture *tx = repository_get_texture(state->repo, texture_id, err);\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&state->lock);\n\n    if (!tx)\n        return NULL; /* Error already populated */\n\n    if (state->metrics)\n        metrics_counter_inc(state->metrics, \"texture_fetched_total\", 1);\n\n    return tx; /* Ownership transferred to caller */\n}\n\n/**\n * Paginated list of textures.  Returns the number of items copied into\n * out_list, or SIZE_MAX on error.\n *\n * The out_list vector is allocated by the caller; this function fills it up to\n * page_req->page_size. Each populated entry must be released with\n * texture_free() by the caller.\n */\nsize_t texture_handler_list(TextureHandler           *handler,\n                            const PaginationRequest  *page_req,\n                            Texture                 **out_list,\n                            TextureError             *err)\n{\n    memset(out_list, 0, sizeof(Texture *) * page_req->page_size);\n\n    TextureHandlerState *state = (TextureHandlerState *)handler;\n    if (!state || !state->ready)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_NOT_INITIALIZED, \"TextureHandler is not initialized\");\n        return SIZE_MAX;\n    }\n\n    if (!page_req || !validation_is_pagination_request_valid(page_req))\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INVALID_ARGUMENT, \"Invalid pagination request\");\n        return SIZE_MAX;\n    }\n\n    if (pthread_rwlock_rdlock(&state->lock) != 0)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INTERNAL, \"Failed to acquire read lock\");\n        return SIZE_MAX;\n    }\n\n    size_t fetched = repository_list_textures(state->repo, page_req, out_list, err);\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&state->lock);\n\n    if (fetched == SIZE_MAX)\n        return SIZE_MAX;\n\n    if (state->metrics)\n        metrics_histogram_observe(state->metrics, \"textures_per_page\", fetched);\n\n    log_debug(\"[texture-handler] Listed %zu textures (page %u)\", fetched, page_req->page_index);\n    return fetched;\n}\n\n/**\n * Deletes a texture by ID.  Returns true on success, false otherwise.\n */\nbool texture_handler_delete(TextureHandler *handler, const char *texture_id, TextureError *err)\n{\n    TextureHandlerState *state = (TextureHandlerState *)handler;\n    if (!state || !state->ready)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_NOT_INITIALIZED, \"TextureHandler is not initialized\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    if (!validation_is_uuid(texture_id))\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INVALID_ARGUMENT, \"Invalid UUID '%s'\", texture_id);\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    if (pthread_rwlock_wrlock(&state->lock) != 0)\n    {\n        _set_error(err, TX_ERR_INTERNAL, \"Failed to acquire write lock\");\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    bool ok = repository_delete_texture(state->repo, texture_id, err);\n    pthread_rwlock_unlock(&state->lock);\n\n    if (ok && state->metrics)\n        metrics_counter_inc(state->metrics, \"texture_deleted_total\", 1);\n\n    log_info(\"[texture-handler] Deleted texture '%s' (%s)\", texture_id, ok ? \"ok\" : \"not-found\");\n    return ok;\n}\n\n/* Written for production use-cases: configuration through\n *   environment variables, structured logging, graceful shutdown, basic\n *   request validation, pagination and thread-safe in-memory storage.\n *\n * Build:\n *   gcc -Wall -Wextra -pedantic -std=c11 \\\n *       -o palette-service main.c -lmicrohttpd -lcjson -lpthread\n *\n * Runtime env-vars:\n *   PAL_SERVICE_PORT   \u2013 listen port (default 8082)\n *   PAL_LOG_LEVEL      \u2013 LOG_DEBUG, LOG_INFO, LOG_WARNING, LOG_ERR (default INFO)\n *\n * Endpoints:\n *   GET  /healthz                       \u2013 liveness probe\n *   GET  /v1/palettes?limit&offset      \u2013 list palettes\n *   POST /v1/palettes                   \u2013 create palette  (see struct Palette spec)\n *   POST /graphql                       \u2013 GraphQL fa\u00e7ade (accepts JSON: {query:\"\"})\n *\n * Copyright (c) 2023-2024\n */\n\n#define _POSIX_C_SOURCE 200809L\n#include <microhttpd.h>\n#include <cjson/cJSON.h>\n\n#include <pthread.h>\n#include <signal.h>\n#include <stdarg.h>\n#include <stdbool.h>\n#include <stdint.h>\n#include <stdio.h>\n#include <stdlib.h>\n#include <string.h>\n#include <syslog.h>\n#include <time.h>\n#include <unistd.h>\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                              Logging helpers                               */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nstatic int CURRENT_LOG_LEVEL = LOG_INFO;\n\n#define LOG(level, fmt, ...)                     \\\n    do {                                         \\\n        if ((level) <= CURRENT_LOG_LEVEL) {      \\\n            syslog(level, fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__);   \\\n        }                                        \\\n    } while (0)\n\n#define LOG_DEBUG(fmt, ...)  LOG(LOG_DEBUG,  fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_INFO_(fmt, ...)  LOG(LOG_INFO,   fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_WARN(fmt, ...)   LOG(LOG_WARNING,fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)\n#define LOG_ERR_(fmt, ...)   LOG(LOG_ERR,    fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__)\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                               Data models                                  */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n#define UUID_LEN        36u\n#define MAX_NAME_LEN   127u\n#define MAX_COLORS       8u   /* maximum colours within a palette           */\n#define MAX_PALETTES  4096u   /* in-memory cap (fits most demo/show-cases)  */\n\ntypedef struct {\n    char     id[UUID_LEN + 1];\n    char     name[MAX_NAME_LEN + 1];\n    char     colors[MAX_COLORS][8];     /* hex colours \u201c#RRGGBB\u201d              */\n    size_t   color_count;\n    time_t   created_at;\n} Palette;\n\ntypedef struct {\n    Palette           *palettes[MAX_PALETTES];\n    size_t             count;\n    pthread_mutex_t    lock;\n} PaletteRepository;\n\n/* Repository instance (singleton inside this process) */\nstatic PaletteRepository g_repo;\n\n/* --------------------- repository (thread-safe) --------------------------- */\nstatic void\nrepo_init(PaletteRepository *repo)\n{\n    memset(repo, 0, sizeof(*repo));\n    pthread_mutex_init(&repo->lock, NULL);\n}\n\nstatic void\nrepo_destroy(PaletteRepository *repo)\n{\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&repo->lock);\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < repo->count; ++i)\n        free(repo->palettes[i]);\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&repo->lock);\n    pthread_mutex_destroy(&repo->lock);\n}\n\nstatic int\nrepo_add(PaletteRepository *repo, const Palette *p_in)\n{\n    int rc = -1;\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&repo->lock);\n    if (repo->count < MAX_PALETTES) {\n        Palette *copy = malloc(sizeof(*copy));\n        if (copy) {\n            *copy = *p_in;\n            repo->palettes[repo->count++] = copy;\n            rc = 0;\n        }\n    }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&repo->lock);\n    return rc;\n}\n\nstatic size_t\nrepo_get_paginated(PaletteRepository *repo,\n                   size_t offset,\n                   size_t limit,\n                   Palette **out_buf,\n                   size_t  buf_len)\n{\n    size_t written = 0;\n\n    pthread_mutex_lock(&repo->lock);\n    if (offset < repo->count) {\n        const size_t avail = repo->count - offset;\n        const size_t n     = (limit < avail ? limit : avail);\n        for (size_t i = 0; i < n && i < buf_len; ++i)\n            out_buf[written++] = repo->palettes[offset + i];\n    }\n    pthread_mutex_unlock(&repo->lock);\n\n    return written;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           Utility functions                                */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/* Very small UUIDv4 generator (pseudo-random).  NOT CRYPTO-SAFE.             */\nstatic void\nuuid_generate(char out[UUID_LEN + 1])\n{\n    static const char *hex = \"0123456789abcdef\";\n    uint8_t rnd[16];\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < sizeof(rnd); ++i)\n        rnd[i] = (uint8_t)(rand() % 256);\n\n    rnd[6] = (rnd[6] & 0x0F) | 0x40; /* version 4 */\n    rnd[8] = (rnd[8] & 0x3F) | 0x80; /* variant 1 */\n\n    snprintf(out, UUID_LEN + 1,\n             \"%02x%02x%02x%02x-\"\n             \"%02x%02x-\"\n             \"%02x%02x-\"\n             \"%02x%02x-\"\n             \"%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x%02x\",\n             rnd[0], rnd[1], rnd[2], rnd[3],\n             rnd[4], rnd[5],\n             rnd[6], rnd[7],\n             rnd[8], rnd[9],\n             rnd[10], rnd[11], rnd[12], rnd[13], rnd[14], rnd[15]);\n}\n\n/* Parse size_t from a string safely; returns default_val on error */\nstatic size_t\nstr_to_sizet(const char *s, size_t default_val)\n{\n    if (!s) return default_val;\n    char *endptr = NULL;\n    unsigned long v = strtoul(s, &endptr, 10);\n    return (endptr != s && *endptr == '\\0') ? (size_t)v : default_val;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                          HTTP / MicroHTTPD layer                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/* Connection specific data used to aggregate POST payloads */\ntypedef struct {\n    char  *body;\n    size_t body_size;\n    size_t body_cap;\n} ConnInfo;\n\nstatic void\nconninfo_free_callback(void *cls, struct MHD_Connection *connection,\n                       void **con_cls, enum MHD_RequestTerminationCode toe)\n{\n    (void)cls; (void)connection; (void)toe;\n    ConnInfo *ci = *con_cls;\n    if (ci) {\n        free(ci->body);\n        free(ci);\n        *con_cls = NULL;\n    }\n}\n\n/* Append incoming data to the buffer, auto-expanding */\nstatic bool\nconninfo_append(ConnInfo *ci, const char *data, size_t size)\n{\n    if (size == 0) return true;\n    if (ci->body_size + size + 1 > ci->body_cap) {\n        size_t new_cap = (ci->body_cap ? ci->body_cap * 2 : 1024);\n        while (new_cap < ci->body_size + size + 1)\n            new_cap *= 2;\n        char *tmp = realloc(ci->body, new_cap);\n        if (!tmp) return false;\n        ci->body      = tmp;\n        ci->body_cap  = new_cap;\n    }\n    memcpy(ci->body + ci->body_size, data, size);\n    ci->body_size += size;\n    ci->body[ci->body_size] = '\\0';\n    return true;\n}\n\n/* --------------------------- REST Handlers -------------------------------- */\nstatic struct MHD_Response *\njson_response(cJSON *json, int status_code)\n{\n    char *json_str = cJSON_PrintUnformatted(json);\n    cJSON_Delete(json);\n    if (!json_str) return NULL;\n\n    struct MHD_Response *resp =\n MHD_add_response_header(resp, \"Connection\", \"close\");\n    return resp;\n}\n\nstatic int\nhandle_healthz(struct MHD_Connection *connection)\n{\n    const char *ok = \"ok\";\n    struct *connection,\n                    const char           *url)\n{\n    (void)url;\n    size_t limit  = str_to_sizet(MHD_lookup_connection_value(connection, MHD_GET_ARGUMENT_KIND, \"limit\"), 10);\n    size_t offset = str_to_sizet(MHD_lookup_connection_value(connection, MHD_GET_ARGUMENT_KIND, \"offset\"), 0);\n\n    if (limit == 0 || limit > 100)\n        limit = 100; /* enforce server-side caps */\n\n    Palette *stack_buf[128]; /* limit capped at 100 so safe */\n    const size_t n = repo_get_paginated(&g_repo, offset, limit, stack_buf, 128);\n\n    cJSON *root  = cJSON_CreateObject();\n    cJSON *items = cJSON_AddArrayToObject(root, \"items\");\n\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < n; ++i) {\n        Palette *p = stack_buf[i];\n        cJSON *jpal = cJSON_CreateObject();\n        cJSON_AddStringToObject(jpal, \"id\", p->id);\n        cJSON_AddStringToObject(jpal, \"name\", p->name);\n        cJSON *col = cJSON_AddArrayToObject(jpal, \"colors\");\n        for (size_t c = 0; c < cJSON_AddItemToArray(items, jpal);\n    }\n    cJSON_AddNumberToObject(root, \"total\", (double)g_repo.count);\n\n    struct MHD_Response *resp = json_response(root, MHD_HTTP_OK);\n    if (!resp) cJSON_GetArraySize(colors);\n    if (color_count == 0 || color_count > MAX_COLORS)\n        goto exit;\n\n    memset(out, 0, sizeof(*out));\n    uuid_generate(out->id);\n    strncpy(out->name, name->valuestring, MAX_NAME_LEN);\n    out->color_count = color_count;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < color_count; ++i) {\n        cJSON *col = cJSON_GetArrayItem(colors, (int)i);\n        if (!cJSON_IsString(col) || strlen(col->valuestring) != 7) /* #RRGGBB */\n            goto exit;\n        strncpy(out->colors[i], col->valuestring, 7);\n    }\n    out->created_at = time(NULL);\n    ok = true;\nexit:\n    cJSON_Delete(root);\n    return ok;\n}\n\nstatic int\nhandle_post_palettes(struct MHD_Connection *connection,\n                     ConnInfo             *ci)\n{\n    Palette p;\n /* abort transfer */\n\n    buf->data = new_data;\n    memcpy(buf->data + buf->size, ptr, bytes);\n    buf->size += bytes;\n    buf->data[buf->size] = '\\0';\n    return bytes;\n}\n\n/* Utility: fatal error & exit */\nstatic void die(const char *msg, CURLcode code)\n{\n    fprintf(stderr, \"ERROR: %s (%s)\\n\", msg, curl_easy_strerror(code));\n    exit(EXIT_FAILURE);\n}\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    static const char *graphql_query =\n        \"{\"\n        \"  currentPalette(page: 1, perPage: 10) {\"\n        \"    id\"\n        \"    name\"\n        \"    colors { hex }\"\n        \"    updatedAt\"\n        \"  }\"\n        \"}\";\n\n    /* JSON body with query */\n    char json_body[1024];\n    snprintf(json_body, sizeof(json_body),\n             \"{\\\"query\\\":\\\"%s\\\"}\", graphql_query);\n\n    /* Initialize curl */\n    CURL *curl = curl_easy_init();\n    if (!curl) {\n        fputs(\"Unable to init curl\\n\", stderr);\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    buffer_t buf = { .data = NULL, .size = 0 };\n\n    /* REST URL fallback; change to https://localhost:8443/graphql for TLS */\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_URL, \"http://localhost:8080/graphql\");\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_HTTP_VERSION, CURL_HTTP_VERSION_2_0);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POST, 1L);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS, json_body);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, on_write);\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, &buf);\n\n    /* Set mandatory headers */\n    struct curl_slist *headers = NULL;\n    headers = curl_slist_append(headers, \"Content-Type: application/json\");\n    headers = curl_slist_append(headers, \"X-SC-Schema-Version: 2024-06\");\n    headers = curl_slist_append(headers, \"X-SC-Request-ID: demo-client-001\");\n    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, headers);\n\n    /* Perform request */\n    CURLcode rc = curl_easy_perform(curl);\n    if (rc != CURLE_OK) die(\"Gateway request failed\", rc);\n\n    /* HTTP status */\n    long code;\n    curl_easy_getinfo(curl, CURLINFO_RESPONSE_CODE, &code);\n    printf(\"HTTP %ld\\n%s\\n\", code, buf.data);\n\n    /* Cleanup */\n    curl_slist_free_all(headers);\n    free(buf.data);\n    curl_easy_cleanup(curl);\n    return 0;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Gateway Highlights\n\nFeature                       | Implementation Details\n------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------\nVersioning                    | `X-SC-Schema-Version` header + Semantic schema directory\nCommand/Query Segregation     | `commands/` (mutations) vs `queries/` (reads) handlers\nRequest Validation            | JSON-Schema & libvalijson; early-reject invalid payloads\nObservability                 | pluggable sinks (stdout, syslog, Loki); OpenTelemetry\nPagination                    | Cursor & offset styles; helpers in `libsc_pagination.a`\nRate Limiting                 | Token bucket (Redis backend) & adaptive load-shedding\nRepository Pattern            | Driver-agnostic adapters (`repo/pg`, `repo/sqlite`, `repo/mock`)\nHot-Reload Schemas            | inotify/FS events \u2192 atomic swap registry\nMemory Safety                 | \u03bcobject memory pool + **ASAN/UBSAN/O2** in CI\n\n---\n\n## 4. because we read sequentially */\n\n    if (feof(ctx->fp))\n        return MHD_CONTENT_READER_END_OF_STREAM;\n\n    size_t n = fread(buf, 1, max < sizeof(ctx->buf) ? max : sizeof(ctx->buf), ctx->fp);\n    if (n == 0)\n        return MHD_CONTENT_READER_END_OF_STREAM;\n\n    return (ssize_t)n;\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Texture synthesis (simple value noise as demonstration)\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------*/\nstatic inline float\nrand_unit(void)\n{\n    return (float)rand() / (float)RAND_MAX;\n}\n\n/* Basic gradient noise (returns value in [0;1]) */\nstatic void\ngenerate_noise_texture(uint32_t width, uint32_t height,\n                       float frequency, uint8_t *out_pixels)\n{\n    for (uint32_t y = 0; y < height; ++y) {\n        for (uint32_t x = 0; x < width; ++x) {\n            float nx = x * frequency;\n            float ny = y * frequency;\n            /* pseudo-random value per pixel */\n            float v = fabsf(sinf(nx * 12.9898f + ny * 78.233f) * 43758.5453f);\n            v = v - floorf(v); /* fract */\n\n            uint8_t c = (uint8_t)(v * 255.0f);\n            size_t idx = ((size_t)y * width + x) * 4;\n            out_pixels[idx + 0] = c;  /* R */\n            out_pixels[idx + 1] = c;  /* G */\n            out_pixels[idx + 2] = c;  /* B */\n            out_pixels[idx + 3] = 255;/* A opaque */\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * LRU Cache\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef struct texture_cache {\n    pthread_mutex_t lock;\n    cache_entry_t  *head; /* MRU */\n    cache_entry_t  *tail; /* NULL,\n    .items = 0,\n    .bytes = 0\n};\n\nstatic void\ncache_move_to_front(cache_entry_t *entry)\n{\n    if (g_cache.head == entry)\n        return;\n\n    /* detach */\n    if (entry->prev)\n        entry->prev->next = entry->next;\n    if (entry->next)\n        entry->next->prev = entry->prev;\n    if (g_cache.tail == entry)\n        g_cache.tail = entry->prev;\n\n    /* insert at front */\n    entry->prev = NULL;\n    entry->next = g_cache.head;\n    if (g_cache.head)\n        g_cache.head->prev = entry;\n    g_cache.head = entry;\n    if (!g_cache.tail)\n        g_cache.tail = entry;\n}\n\nstatic cache_entry_t *\ncache_find(const char *id)\n{\n    cache_entry_t *it = g_cache.head;\n    while (it) {\n        if (strcmp(it->meta.id, id) == 0)\n            return it;\n        it = it->next;\n    }\n    return NULL;\n}\n\nstatic void\ncache_evict_if_needed(void)\n{\n    while (g_cache.items > MAX_CACHE_ITEMS) {\n        cache_entry_t *victim = g_cache.tail;\n        if (!victim)\n            return;\n        /* detach */\n        if (victim->prev)\n            victim->prev->next = NULL;\n        g_cache.tail = victim->prev;\n        if (g_cache.head == victim)\n            g_cache.head = NULL;\n\n        g_cache.items--;\n        g_cache.bytes -= victim->size;\n        LOG_INFO(\"Evicted texture %s from cache (now %\" PRIu64 \" KiB)\",\n                 victim->meta.id, (uint64_t)(g_cache.bytes / 1024));\n\n        free(victim->pixels);\n        free(victim);\n    }\n}\n\nstatic void\ncache_insert(cache_entry_t *entry)\n{\n    entry->prev = NULL;\n    entry->next = g_cache.head;\n    if (g_cache.head)\n        g_cache.head->prev = entry;\n    g_cache.head = entry;\n    if (!g_cache.tail)\n        g_cache.tail = entry;\n\n    g_cache.items++;\n    g_cache.bytes += entry->size;\n    cache_evict_if_needed();\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * REST Controller helpers\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------*/\ntypedef struct rest_ctx {\n    struct MHD_Connection *conn;\n    const char            *url;\n    const char            *method;\n} rest_ctx_t;\n\nstatic int\nresp_json(struct MHD_Connection *conn, unsigned status,\n          const char *json_str)\n{\n    struct MHD_Response *resp = MHD_create_response_from_buffer(\n        strlen(json_str), (void *)json_str, MHD_RESPMEM_MUST_COPY);\n    if (!resp)\n        return MHD_NO;\n\n    MHD_add_response_header(resp, \"Content-Type\", \"application/json\");\n    int ret = MHD_queue_response(conn, status, resp);\n    MHD_destroy_response(resp);\n    return ret;\n}\n\nstatic int\nresp_plain(struct MHD_Connection *conn, unsigned status,\n           const char *text)\n{\n    struct MHD_Response *resp = MHD_create_response_from_buffer(\n        strlen(text), (void *)text, MHD_RESPMEM_MUST_COPY);\n    if (!resp)\n        return MHD_NO;\n\n    MHD_add_response_header(resp, \"Content-Type\", \"text/plain\");\n    int ret = MHD_queue_response(conn, status, resp);\n    MHD_destroy_response(resp);\n    return ret;\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n * Endpoint: POST /textures\n * Body (form-encoded):\n *   width=<int>&height=<int>&freq=<float>\n * Returns JSON: { \"id\": \"...\", \"width\": n, \"height\": n }\n * ----------------------------------------------------------------------*/\nstatic int\nhandle_post_textures(rest_ctx_t *ctx)\n{\n    uint32_t width  = 0, height = 0;\n    float freq = DEFAULT_NOISE_FREQ;\n\n    const char *width_str  = MHD_lookup_connection_value(ctx->conn, MHD_POST_FIELD_KIND, \"width\");\n    const char *height_str = MHD_lookup_connection_value(ctx->conn, MHD_POST_FIELD_KIND, \"height\");\n    const char *freq_str   = MHD_lookup_connection_value(ctx->conn, MHD_POST_FIELD_KIND, \"freq\");\n\n    if (width_str)  width  = (uint32_t)strtoul(width_str, NULL, 10);\n    if (height_str) height = (uint32_t)strtoul(height_str, NULL, 10);\n    if (freq_str)   freq   = strtof(freq_str, NULL);\n\n    if (width == 0 || height == 0 || width > MAX_TEXTURE_SIDE || height > MAX_TEXTURE_SIDE) {\n        return resp_plain(ctx->conn, MHD_HTTP_BAD_REQUEST, \"Invalid dimensions\");\n    }\n\n    size_t bytes = (size_t)width * height * 4;\n    uint8_t *pixels = malloc(bytes);\n    if (!pixels)\n        return resp_plain(ctx->conn, MHD_HTTP_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR, \"OOM\");\n\n    generate_noise_texture(width, height, freq,  syslog(LOG_ERR, \"failed to load configuration; exiting\");\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    curl_global_init(CURL_GLOBAL_DEFAULT);\n\n    struct MHD_Daemon *d = MHD_start_daemon(\n                                MHD_USE_THREAD_POOL | MHD_USE_TCP_FASTOPEN,\n                                cfg->port,\n                                NULL, NULL,\n                                &access_handler_cb, cfg,\n                                MHD_OPTION_THREAD_POOL_SIZE, HTTP_THREAD_POOL,\n                                MHD_OPTION_END);\n    if (!d) {\n        syslog(LOG_ERR, \"failed to start HTTP daemon on port %u\", cfg->port);\n        conf_free(cfg);\n        return EXIT_FAILURE;\n    }\n\n    syslog(LOG_INFO, \"gateway started on port %u\", cfg->port);\n\n    signal(SIGINT, sigint_handler);\n    signal(SIGTERM, sigint_handler);\n\n    while (g_running) {\n        pause();\n    }\n\n    syslog(LOG_INFO, \"shutting down\");\n    MHD_stop_daemon(d);\n    curl_global_cleanup();\n    conf_free(cfg);\n    closelog();\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```",
