  "content": "# Technical Report: Migration from Custom IPC to gRPC\n\n## SynestheticCanvas API Suite - Inter-Service Communication Migration Analysis\n\n**Author:** Principal Engineer\n**Date:** 2026-02-02\n**Version:** 1.0\n\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis report provides a comprehensive technical analysis of migrating the SynestheticCanvas API Suite from its current custom Inter-Process Communication (IPC) library (`sc_ipc`) to gRPC. The analysis covers component identification, data flow analysis, a phased migration strategy, and risk assessment. The migration is deemed feasible with careful planning, particularly around build system modifications and a parallel deployment strategy to ensure zero-downtime transitions.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Component Identification: Current IPC System\n\n### 1.1 Shared IPC Library (`sc_ipc`)\n\nThe core inter-service communication is built on a custom UNIX domain socket-based IPC library.\n\n| Component | Path | Description |\n|-----------|------|-------------|\n| **Header** | `libs/sc_ipc/include/sc_ipc.h` | Public API definitions, error codes, message types |\n| **Implementation** | `libs/sc_ipc/src/sc_ipc.c` | Socket management, message framing, send/recv operations |\n\n**Key API Functions (from `sc_ipc.h`):**\n\n```c\n// Server-side initialization\nint sc_ipc_server_init(sc_ipc_channel_t *srv, const char *endpoint, size_t backlog);\nint sc_ipc_accept(const sc_ipc_channel_t *srv, sc_ipc_channel_t *out_cli, uint32_t timeout_ms);\n\n// Client-side initialization\nint sc_ipc_client_init(sc_ipc_channel_t *cli, const char *endpoint, uint32_t timeout_ms);\n\n// Message I/O\nint sc_ipc_send_msg(sc_ipc_channel_t *chan, sc_ipc_msg_type_t type, const void *payload,\n                    size_t payload_len, uint64_t correlation_id, uint32_t timeout_ms);\nint sc_ipc_recv_msg(sc_ipc_channel_t *chan, sc_ipc_msg_hdr_t *hdr, void *buf,\n                    size_t buf_size, uint32_t timeout_ms);\n\n// Cleanup\nvoid sc_ipc_close(sc_ipc_channel_t *chan);\n```\n\n**Protocol Characteristics:**\n- Transport: UNIX domain sockets (AF_UNIX)\n- Framing: Length-prefixed (4-byte big-endian header)\n- Maximum payload: 64 KiB (`SC_IPC_MAX_PAYLOAD`)\n- Message types: REQUEST, RESPONSE, EVENT, HEARTBEAT\n- Correlation ID support for request/response matching\n\n### 1.2 API Gateway Client-Side Implementation\n\n| Component | Path | Description |\n|-----------|------|-------------|\n| **Service Client** | `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` | HTTP/REST client wrapper using libcurl |\n| **GraphQL Resolvers** | `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c` | GraphQL resolver implementations calling backend services |\n| **Gateway Server** | `api-gateway/src/gateway_server.c` | Main gateway entry point with proxying logic |\n\n**Current Communication Pattern:**\nThe API Gateway currently uses **HTTP/REST over libcurl** rather than the raw `sc_ipc` library for inter-service communication. The `service_client.c` (lines 174-198) implements:\n\n```c\nint sc_service_client_call(sc_service_client_t *cli,\n                           sc_service_endp_t    endpoint,\n                           const char          *method,\n                           const char          *path,\n                           const char          *request_json,\n                           cJSON              **response_json,\n                           long                *http_status);\n```\n\n**Service Endpoint Configuration (from `service_client.c`, lines 41-44):**\n- `SC_PALETTE_SERVICE_URL` - Palette service base URL\n- `SC_TEXTURE_SERVICE_URL` - Texture service base URL\n- `SC_AUDIO_SERVICE_URL` - Audio service base URL\n- `SC_NARRATIVE_SERVICE_URL` - Narrative service base URL\n\n### 1.3 Backend Microservice Implementations\n\n| Service | Main Entry Point | Handler | Port |\n|---------|-----------------|---------|------|\n| **Texture Service** | `services/texture-service/src/main.c` | `services/texture-service/src/texture_handler.c` | 7002 |\n| **Palette Service** | `services/palette-service/src/main.c` | N/A (inline) | 7001 |\n| **Audio Service** | `services/audio-service/src/main.c` | TBD | 7003 |\n| **Narrative Service** | `services/narrative-service/src/main.c` | TBD | 7004 |\n\n**Current Backend HTTP Server Implementation:**\nAll microservices use **libmicrohttpd** for HTTP serving. From `texture-service/src/main.c` (lines 415-421):\n\n```c\nsvc.daemon = MHD_start_daemon(MHD_USE_AUTO | MHD_USE_INTERNAL_POLLING_THREAD,\n                              svc.cfg.port,\n                              NULL, NULL,\n                              request_router, &svc,\n                              MHD_OPTION_CONNECTION_TIMEOUT, (unsigned int)10,\n                              MHD_OPTION_END);\n```\n\n### 1.4 Common Libraries\n\n| Library | Path | Purpose |\n|---------|------|---------|\n| **sc_common** | `libs/sc_common/` | Shared configuration, logging, error handling |\n| **sc_config.h** | `libs/sc_common/include/sc_config.h` | Runtime configuration structures |\n| **sc_logging.h** | `libs/sc_common/include/sc_logging.h` | Structured logging facade |\n| **sc_errors.h** | `libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h` | Error code definitions |\n\n### 1.5 Build System Files\n\n| Component | Path | Modifications Required |\n|-----------|------|----------------------|\n| **Root CMake** | `CMakeLists.txt` | Add gRPC/Protobuf dependencies |\n| **Gateway CMake** | `api-gateway/CMakeLists.txt` | Link gRPC libraries, add proto compilation |\n| **Texture Service CMake** | `services/texture-service/CMakeLists.txt` | Add gRPC server support |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Data Flow Analysis\n\n### 2.1 Current Request Flow (Based on `data_flow.puml`)\n\nThe PlantUML diagram (`docs/architecture/data_flow.puml`) illustrates the following synchronous request path:\n\n```\nClient \u2192 API Gateway \u2192 Rate Limiter \u2192 Redis Cache \u2192 Request Validator \u2192 GraphQL Resolver\n                                                                              \u2193\n                                                                    [Texture Service]\n                                                                              \u2193\n                                                                    PostgreSQL/Redis\n                                                                              \u2193\n                                                                    Response \u2190 Client\n```\n\n### 2.2 Detailed Request Flow: API Gateway to Texture Service\n\n#### Step 1: Client Request Arrival\n**File:** `api-gateway/src/gateway_server.c` (lines 390-468)\n\n```c\nstatic int access_handler_cb(void *cls, struct MHD_Connection *conn,\n                             const char *url, const char *method, ...)\n```\n\n1. Request received by libmicrohttpd\n2. Rate limiting check via token bucket (`rate_limit_get_bucket()`)\n3. URL routing to appropriate handler\n\n#### Step 2: GraphQL Resolution\n**File:** `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c` (lines 184-210)\n\n```c\nstatic json_t *resolve_palette(const json_t *args, void *user_data, GQLError **gql_err)\n{\n    // Extract arguments\n    const char *id = json_string_value(json_object_get(args, \"id\"));\n\n    // Rate limit check\n    if (rate_limiter_acquire(ctx->limiter) != 0) { ... }\n\n    // Build upstream URL\n    char url[512];\n    snprintf(url, sizeof(url), \"%s/palettes/%s\", PALETTE_SERVICE_BASE_URL, id);\n\n    // Call upstream service via HTTP\n    json_t *payload = http_json_get(url, ctx->log, gql_err);\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Service Client Call\n**File:** `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` (lines 247-330)\n\n```c\nstatic int perform_request(sc_service_client_t *client, const char *url,\n                           const char *method, const char *json_body,\n                           long *http_status, cJSON **out_body)\n{\n    // Uses libcurl for HTTP communication\n    curl_easy_setopt(h, CURLOPT_URL, url);\n    curl_easy_setopt(h, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, hdrs);\n    res = curl_easy_perform(h);\n}\n```\n\n**Key Data Structures:**\n- `sc_service_client_t` - Client state with per-service URLs, metrics\n- `response_buf_t` - Dynamic response buffer\n- Request/response serialization via **cJSON**\n\n#### Step 4: Texture Service Processing\n**File:** `services/texture-service/src/main.c` (lines 347-378)\n\n```c\nstatic enum MHD_Result request_router(void *cls, struct MHD_Connection *connection,\n                                      const char *url, const char *method, ...)\n{\n    if (strcmp(url, \"/healthz\") == 0) {\n        return handle_healthz(connection);\n    }\n    else if (strcmp(url, \"/v1/noise\") == 0) {\n        return handle_noise(svc, connection);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Handler Processing:**\n**File:** `services/texture-service/src/texture_handler.c` (lines 132-194)\n\n```c\nTexture *texture_handler_create(TextureHandler *handler, const TextureInput *input,\n                                TextureError *err)\n{\n    // Validation\n    if (!_validate_texture_input(input, err)) return NULL;\n\n    // Build domain object\n    tx.id = _generate_uuid();\n\n    // Repository persistence\n    bool persist_ok = repository_save_texture(state->repo, &tx, err);\n\n    // Metrics update\n    if (state->metrics) metrics_counter_inc(state->metrics, \"texture_created_total\", 1);\n\n    return texture_clone(&tx, err);\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 5: Response Path\n\n1. Handler returns JSON response via `MHD_create_response_from_buffer()`\n2. Response flows back through libmicrohttpd\n3. Gateway receives HTTP response via libcurl\n4. Gateway parses JSON via `cJSON_Parse()`\n5. GraphQL resolver returns payload to client\n\n---\n\n## 3. Migration Strategy Proposal\n\n### 3.1 Overview: Phased Migration Approach\n\nThe migration will follow a **strangler fig pattern** with parallel systems operating simultaneously. This ensures zero downtime and allows for gradual rollout with easy rollback capability.\n\n```\nPhase 1: Infrastructure Setup (gRPC dependencies, proto definitions)\n    \u2193\nPhase 2: Texture Service Dual-Protocol Support (gRPC + HTTP)\n    \u2193\nPhase 3: API Gateway gRPC Client Integration (Feature Flag)\n    \u2193\nPhase 4: Traffic Migration (Gradual rollout)\n    \u2193\nPhase 5: Legacy HTTP Deprecation & Removal\n```\n\n### 3.2 Phase 1: Infrastructure Setup\n\n#### 3.2.1 Protocol Buffer Definition\n\n**New File:** `protos/texture.proto`\n\n```protobuf\nsyntax = \"proto3\";\n\npackage synestheticcanvas.texture.v1;\n\noption c_enable_arenas = true;\n\nservice TextureService {\n    rpc CreateTexture(CreateTextureRequest) returns (CreateTextureResponse);\n    rpc GetTexture(GetTextureRequest) returns (GetTextureResponse);\n    rpc ListTextures(ListTexturesRequest) returns (ListTexturesResponse);\n    rpc DeleteTexture(DeleteTextureRequest) returns (DeleteTextureResponse);\n    rpc GetTextureRaw(GetTextureRawRequest) returns (stream TextureChunk);\n}\n\nmessage CreateTextureRequest {\n    string name = 1;\n    string color_profile = 2;\n    uint32 width = 3;\n    uint32 height = 4;\n    float frequency = 5;\n}\n\nmessage CreateTextureResponse {\n    string id = 1;\n    uint32 width = 2;\n    uint32 height = 3;\n    string created_at = 4;\n}\n\nmessage GetTextureRequest {\n    string id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage GetTextureResponse {\n    string id = 1;\n    string name = 2;\n    string color_profile = 3;\n    uint32 width = 4;\n    uint32 height = 5;\n    string created_at = 6;\n}\n\nmessage ListTexturesRequest {\n    uint32 page_size = 1;\n    string page_token = 2;\n}\n\nmessage ListTexturesResponse {\n    repeated GetTextureResponse textures = 1;\n    string next_page_token = 2;\n    uint32 total_count = 3;\n}\n\nmessage DeleteTextureRequest {\n    string id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage DeleteTextureResponse {\n    bool success = 1;\n}\n\nmessage GetTextureRawRequest {\n    string id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage TextureChunk {\n    bytes data = 1;\n    uint64 offset = 2;\n    uint64 total_size = 3;\n}\n```\n\n#### 3.2.2 Root CMakeLists.txt Modifications\n\n**File:** `CMakeLists.txt` (Add after line 127)\n\n```cmake\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#  gRPC and Protocol Buffers Support\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\noption(SC_ENABLE_GRPC \"Enable gRPC support for inter-service communication\" OFF)\n\nif(SC_ENABLE_GRPC)\n    find_package(Protobuf REQUIRED)\n    find_package(gRPC REQUIRED)\n\n    # Locate grpc_cpp_plugin for code generation\n    find_program(GRPC_CPP_PLUGIN grpc_cpp_plugin REQUIRED)\n\n    # Proto compilation function\n    function(add_proto_library TARGET_NAME PROTO_FILE)\n        get_filename_component(PROTO_PATH ${PROTO_FILE} DIRECTORY)\n        get_filename_component(PROTO_NAME ${PROTO_FILE} NAME_WE)\n\n        set(PROTO_SRCS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.pb.c\")\n        set(PROTO_HDRS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.pb.h\")\n        set(GRPC_SRCS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.grpc.pb.c\")\n        set(GRPC_HDRS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.grpc.pb.h\")\n\n        add_custom_command(\n            OUTPUT ${PROTO_SRCS} ${PROTO_HDRS} ${GRPC_SRCS} ${GRPC_HDRS}\n            COMMAND protobuf::protoc\n            ARGS --proto_path=${PROTO_PATH}\n                 --c_out=${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}\n                 --grpc_out=${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}\n                 --plugin=protoc-gen-grpc=${GRPC_CPP_PLUGIN}\n                 ${PROTO_FILE}\n            DEPENDS ${PROTO_FILE}\n        )\n\n        add_library(${TARGET_NAME} STATIC ${PROTO_SRCS} ${GRPC_SRCS})\n        target_include_directories(${TARGET_NAME} PUBLIC ${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR})\n        target_link_libraries(${TARGET_NAME} PUBLIC protobuf::libprotobuf-c gRPC::grpc)\n    endfunction()\n\n    # Compile proto files\n    add_proto_library(texture_proto ${PROJECT_SOURCE_DIR}/protos/texture.proto)\nendif()\n```\n\n### 3.3 Phase 2: Texture Service Dual-Protocol Support\n\nThe texture service will be modified to listen on **two ports simultaneously**: one for the existing HTTP/REST API and one for gRPC.\n\n#### 3.3.1 Texture Service CMakeLists.txt Modifications\n\n**File:** `services/texture-service/CMakeLists.txt` (Add after line 157)\n\n```cmake\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#  gRPC Server Support (Optional)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\noption(TEXTURESVC_ENABLE_GRPC \"Enable gRPC server endpoint\" OFF)\n\nif(TEXTURESVC_ENABLE_GRPC)\n    if(NOT TARGET texture_proto)\n        message(FATAL_ERROR \"texture_proto target not found. Build with -DSC_ENABLE_GRPC=ON\")\n    endif()\n\n    target_sources(texture_service PRIVATE\n        src/grpc_server.c\n        src/grpc_handlers.c\n    )\n\n    target_link_libraries(texture_service\n        PRIVATE\n            texture_proto\n            gRPC::grpc\n            gRPC::grpc++\n    )\n\n    target_compile_definitions(texture_service PRIVATE ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER=1)\nendif()\n```\n\n#### 3.3.2 Dual-Protocol Main Entry Point\n\n**New File:** `services/texture-service/src/grpc_server.c`\n\n```c\n/**\n * gRPC Server implementation for Texture Service\n * Runs alongside HTTP server for parallel protocol support\n */\n\n#include <grpc/grpc.h>\n#include <grpc/support/log.h>\n#include \"texture.grpc.pb-c.h\"\n#include \"texture_handler.h\"\n\n#define GRPC_DEFAULT_PORT 17002  // gRPC on separate port\n\ntypedef struct {\n    grpc_server *server;\n    grpc_completion_queue *cq;\n    TextureHandler *handler;\n    volatile bool running;\n} grpc_texture_server_t;\n\n// gRPC service method implementations\nstatic void handle_create_texture(grpc_texture_server_t *srv,\n                                  const CreateTextureRequest *req,\n                                  CreateTextureResponse *resp) {\n    TextureInput input = {\n        .name = req->name,\n        .color_profile = req->color_profile,\n        .width = req->width,\n        .height = req->height\n    };\n\n    TextureError err = {0};\n    Texture *tx = texture_handler_create(srv->handler, &input, &err);\n\n    if (tx) {\n        resp->id = strdup(tx->id);\n        resp->width = tx->width;\n        resp->height = tx->height;\n        // Format timestamp\n        char ts[32];\n        strftime(ts, sizeof(ts), \"%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ\", gmtime(&tx->created_at));\n        resp->created_at = strdup(ts);\n        texture_free(tx);\n    }\n}\n\ngrpc_texture_server_t *grpc_texture_server_create(TextureHandler *handler, uint16_t port);\nvoid grpc_texture_server_serve(grpc_texture_server_t *srv);\nvoid grpc_texture_server_stop(grpc_texture_server_t *srv);\nvoid grpc_texture_server_destroy(grpc_texture_server_t *srv);\n```\n\n#### 3.3.3 Modified main.c for Dual-Protocol\n\n**File:** `services/texture-service/src/main.c` (Modifications)\n\n```c\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER\n#include \"grpc_server.h\"\n#include <pthread.h>\n\nstatic pthread_t g_grpc_thread;\nstatic grpc_texture_server_t *g_grpc_server = NULL;\n\nstatic void *grpc_server_thread(void *arg) {\n    grpc_texture_server_t *srv = (grpc_texture_server_t *)arg;\n    grpc_texture_server_serve(srv);\n    return NULL;\n}\n#endif\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    ServiceCtx svc;\n    config_set_defaults(&svc.cfg);\n\n    // ... existing HTTP setup ...\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER\n    // Start gRPC server on separate port\n    uint16_t grpc_port = (uint16_t)sc_u16_from_env(\"TEXTURE_GRPC_PORT\", 17002);\n    g_grpc_server = grpc_texture_server_create(svc.handler, grpc_port);\n    if (g_grpc_server) {\n        pthread_create(&g_grpc_thread, NULL, grpc_server_thread, g_grpc_server);\n        log_msg(LOG_INFO, \"gRPC server started on port %u\", grpc_port);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    // Start HTTP daemon (existing code)\n    svc.daemon = MHD_start_daemon(...);\n\n    while (!g_shutdown)\n        sleep(1);\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER\n    if (g_grpc_server) {\n        grpc_texture_server_stop(g_grpc_server);\n        pthread_join(g_grpc_thread, NULL);\n        grpc_texture_server_destroy(g_grpc_server);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    MHD_stop_daemon(svc.daemon);\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```\n\n### 3.4 Phase 3: API Gateway gRPC Client Integration\n\n#### 3.4.1 Gateway CMakeLists.txt Modifications\n\n**File:** `api-gateway/CMakeLists.txt` (Add after line 147)\n\n```cmake\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#  gRPC Client Support\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\noption(GATEWAY_ENABLE_GRPC \"Enable gRPC client for upstream services\" OFF)\n\nif(GATEWAY_ENABLE_GRPC)\n    if(NOT TARGET texture_proto)\n        message(FATAL_ERROR \"texture_proto target not found.   texture_proto\n            gRPC::grpc\n    )\n\n    target_compile_definitions(api_gateway PRIVATE ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT=1)\nendif()\n```\n\n#### 3.4.2 Feature Flag for Protocol Selection\n\n**File:** `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` (Modifications)\n\n```c\n// Add to sc_service_client_t structure\nstruct sc_service_client\n{\n    // ... existing fields ...\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT\n    /* gRPC channels */\n    grpc_channel *texture_grpc_channel;\n    bool use_grpc_texture;  // Feature flag\n#endif\n};\n\n// Modified initialization\nsc_service_client_t *sc_service_client_new(void)\n{\n    // ... existing code ...\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT\n    // Check feature flag\n    cli->use_grpc_texture = sc_bool_from_env(\"SC_USE_GRPC_TEXTURE\", false);\n\n    if (cli->use_grpc_texture) {\n        const char *grpc_addr = getenv(\"SC_TEXTURE_GRPC_URL\") ?: \"texture-service:17002\";\n        cli->texture_grpc_channel = grpc_insecure_channel_create(grpc_addr, NULL, NULL);\n        LOG_INF(\"gRPC enabled for texture service: %s\", grpc_addr);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    return cli;\n}\n\n// Modified call function\nint sc_service_client_call(sc_service_client_t *cli,\n                           sc_service_endp_t    endpoint,\n                           const char          *method,\n                           const char          *path,\n                           const char          *request_json,\n                           cJSON              **response_json,\n                           long                *http_status)\n{\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT\n    if (endpoint == SC_EP_TEXTURE && cli->use_grpc_texture) {\n        return sc_service_client_call_grpc(cli, path, request_json,\n                                           response_json, http_status);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    // Fall back to HTTP\n    return sc_service_client_call_http(cli, endpoint, method, path,\n                                       request_json, response_json, http_status);\n}\n```\n\n### 3.5 Phase 4: Traffic Migration Strategy\n\n#### 3.5.1 Deployment Configuration\n\n**Modified docker-compose.yml:**\n\n```yaml\ntexture_service:\n  environment:\n    <<: *default-env\n    SERVICE_PORT: 7002\n    TEXTURE_GRPC_PORT: 17002  # New gRPC port\n  ports:\n    - \"7002:7002\"    # HTTP (existing)\n    - \"17002:17002\"  # gRPC (new)\n\napi_gateway:\n  environment:\n    <<: *default-env\n    SC_USE_GRPC_TEXTURE: \"false\"  # Start with HTTP\n    SC_TEXTURE_GRPC_URL: \"texture_service:17002\"\n```\n\n#### 3.5.2 Gradual Rollout Process\n\n1. **Week 1:** Deploy texture service with dual-protocol support\n   - Monitor gRPC health endpoint\n   - Verify no performance degradation\n\n2. **Week 2:** Enable gRPC for internal testing\n   ```bash\n   export SC_USE_GRPC_TEXTURE=true  # On test gateway instances\n   ```\n\n3. **Week 3:** Canary deployment (5% traffic)\n   - Use load balancer weighted routing\n   - Monitor error rates and latency\n\n4. **Week 4:** Gradual increase (25% \u2192 50% \u2192 100%)\n\n5. **Week 5:** Deprecate HTTP endpoints (keep for rollback)\n\n### 3.6 Phase 5: Legacy HTTP Deprecation\n\nAfter successful migration:\n\n1. Remove HTTP endpoints from texture service\n2. Remove HTTP client code from gateway\n3. Update CMakeLists.txt to make gRPC the default\n4. Remove feature flags\n\n---\n\n## 4. Risk Assessment\n\n### 4.1 Risk 1: Build System Complexity\n\n**Severity:** HIGH\n**Likelihood:** HIGH\n\n**Description:**\nAdding gRPC to a pure C project introduces significant build system complexity. gRPC's C implementation requires:\n- Protocol Buffers compiler and runtime (`protobuf-c`)\n- gRPC C core library (`grpc`)\n- C++ toolchain (gRPC core has C++ dependencies)\n\n**Evidence:**\nCurrent CMakeLists.txt uses pure C with `-std=c17` standard (see `api-gateway/CMakeLists.txt`, line 66). gRPC-C requires linking against C++ runtime.\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Use `grpc` C-core library instead of `grpc++`\n- Consider using `protobuf-c` for pure C protobuf support\n- Provide comprehensive Docker build images with pre-installed dependencies\n- Implement FetchContent fallbacks for missing system packages\n\n### 4.2 Risk 2: Performance Regression\n\n**Severity:** MEDIUM\n**Likelihood:** MEDIUM\n\n**Description:**\nThe current custom IPC uses UNIX domain sockets with minimal framing overhead (4-byte length prefix). gRPC introduces HTTP/2 framing overhead, protobuf serialization, and TLS handshakes (if enabled).\n\n**Evidence:**\nFrom `libs/sc_ipc/src/sc_ipc.c` (line 315-340), the current protocol uses simple `writev()` syscalls with minimal overhead.\n\n**Performance Characteristics Comparison:**\n\n| Aspect | Custom IPC | gRPC (HTTP/2) |\n|--------|-----------|---------------|\n| Framing overhead | 4 bytes | ~20-50 bytes |\n| Serialization | JSON/raw | Protobuf (binary) |\n| Connection setup | None (UNIX socket) | TCP + HTTP/2 handshake |\n| Latency (typical) | <1ms | 1-5ms |\n| Throughput | Higher | Lower (due to framing) |\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Enable gRPC keep-alive to reduce connection overhead\n- Use streaming for large payloads (texture data)\n- Consider Unix Domain Socket transport for gRPC (if same host)\n- Benchmark before and after migration\n\n### 4.3 Risk 3: Operational Complexity During Transition\n\n**Severity:** MEDIUM\n**Likelihood:** HIGH\n\n**Description:**\nRunning a hybrid system with both HTTP and gRPC endpoints increases operational burden:\n- Doubled port exposure and monitoring\n- Complex debugging (two protocols)\n- Inconsistent behavior during transition\n\n**Evidence:**\nDocker-compose configuration shows services already expose multiple ports (see `docker-compose.yml`, lines 59-61).\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Unified observability (OpenTelemetry supports both HTTP and gRPC)\n- Single health check endpoint covering both protocols\n- Clear runbooks for protocol-specific troubleshooting\n- Automated testing for both code paths\n\n### 4.4 Risk 4: Serialization Compatibility\n\n**Severity:** MEDIUM\n**Likelihood:** LOW\n\n**Description:**\nThe current system uses JSON for all payloads. Migration to Protobuf requires careful schema definition to maintain backward compatibility.\n\n**Evidence:**\nFrom `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c` (line 125), responses are parsed with `json_loads()`. From `services/texture-service/src/texture_handler.c` (line 373-394), JSON serialization is used throughout.\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Define protobuf schemas that map 1:1 with existing JSON\n- Add `json_name` options for field name compatibility\n- Maintain JSON gateway for external consumers\n- Version protobuf schemas from the start\n\n### 4.5 Risk 5: Debugging and Observability\n\n**Severity:** LOW\n**Likelihood:** MEDIUM\n\n**Description:**\nJSON payloads are human-readable and easy to debug. Protobuf binary encoding requires additional tooling.\n\n**Evidence:**\nCurrent logging in `service_client.c` (lines 337-354) outputs JSON directly to stderr.\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Use gRPC reflection service for introspection\n- Implement protobuf-to-JSON logging adapter\n- Use `grpcurl` or similar tools for debugging\n- Enable gRPC verbose logging during development\n\n---\n\n## 5. New gRPC-Based Communication Flow\n\n### 5.1 Request Flow Diagram\n\n```\n Conclusion\n\nThe migration from custom IPC to gRPC is technically feasible and will provide significant benefits:\n\n**Benefits:**\n- Standardized interface definitions (Protocol Buffers)\n- Language-agnostic service contracts\n- Built-in streaming support for large payloads\n- Rich ecosystem (reflection, health checks, load balancing)\n- Better tooling for debugging and testing\n\n**Recommended Approach:**\n1. Start with the texture service as a pilot\n2. Use parallel protocol deployment (no big-bang cutover)\n3. Feature flag-controlled gradual rollout\n4. Maintain HTTP fallback for rollback capability\n\n**Timeline Estimate:**\n- Phase 1 (Infrastructure): 2-3 weeks\n- Phase 2 (Texture Service): 2-3 weeks\n- Phase 3 (Gateway Client): 2 weeks\n- Phase 4 (Migration): 4-6 weeks\n- Phase 5 (Cleanup): 1-2 weeks\n\n**Total:** 11-16 weeks for complete migration\n\n---\n\n## 7.   "content": "# Technical Report: Migration from Custom IPC to gRPC\n\n## SynestheticCanvas API Suite - Inter-Service Communication Migration Analysis\n\n**Author:** Principal Engineer\n**Date:** 2026-02-02\n**Version:** 1.0\n\n---\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis report provides a comprehensive technical analysis of migrating the SynestheticCanvas API Suite from its current custom Inter-Process Communication (IPC) library (`sc_ipc`) to gRPC. The analysis covers component identification, data flow analysis, a phased migration strategy, and risk assessment. The migration is deemed feasible with careful planning, particularly around build system modifications and a parallel deployment strategy to ensure zero-downtime transitions.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Component Identification: Current IPC System\n\n### 1.1 Shared IPC Library (`sc_ipc`)\n\nThe core inter-service communication is built on a custom UNIX domain socket-based IPC library.\n\n| Component | Path | Description |\n|-----------|------|-------------|\n| **Header** | `libs/sc_ipc/include/sc_ipc.h` | Public API definitions, error codes, message types |\n| **Implementation** | `libs/sc_ipc/src/sc_ipc.c` | Socket management, message framing, send/recv operations |\n\n**Key API Functions (from `sc_ipc.h`):**\n\n```c\n// Server-side initialization\nint sc_ipc_server_init(sc_ipc_channel_t *srv, const char *endpoint, size_t backlog);\nint sc_ipc_accept(const sc_ipc_channel_t *srv, sc_ipc_channel_t *out_cli, uint32_t timeout_ms);\n\n// Client-side initialization\nint sc_ipc_client_init(sc_ipc_channel_t *cli, const char *endpoint, uint32_t timeout_ms);\n\n// Message I/O\nint sc_ipc_send_msg(sc_ipc_channel_t *chan, sc_ipc_msg_type_t type, const void *payload,\n                    size_t payload_len, uint64_t correlation_id, uint32_t timeout_ms);\nint sc_ipc_recv_msg(sc_ipc_channel_t *chan, sc_ipc_msg_hdr_t *hdr, void *buf,\n                    size_t buf_size, uint32_t timeout_ms);\n\n// Cleanup\nvoid sc_ipc_close(sc_ipc_channel_t *chan);\n```\n\n**Protocol Characteristics:**\n- Transport: UNIX domain sockets (AF_UNIX)\n- Framing: Length-prefixed (4-byte big-endian header)\n- Maximum payload: 64 KiB (`SC_IPC_MAX_PAYLOAD`)\n- Message types: REQUEST, RESPONSE, EVENT, HEARTBEAT\n- Correlation ID support for request/response matching\n\n### 1.2 API Gateway Client-Side Implementation\n\n| Component | Path | Description |\n|-----------|------|-------------|\n| **Service Client** | `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` | HTTP/REST client wrapper using libcurl |\n| **GraphQL Resolvers** | `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c` | GraphQL resolver implementations calling backend services |\n| **Gateway Server** | `api-gateway/src/gateway_server.c` | Main gateway entry point with proxying logic |\n\n**Current Communication Pattern:**\nThe API Gateway currently uses **HTTP/REST over libcurl** rather than the raw `sc_ipc` library for inter-service communication. The `service_client.c` (lines 174-198) implements:\n\n```c\nint sc_service_client_call(sc_service_client_t *cli,\n                           sc_service_endp_t    endpoint,\n                           const char          *method,\n                           const char          *path,\n                           const char          *request_json,\n                           cJSON              **response_json,\n                           long                *http_status);\n```\n\n**Service Endpoint Configuration (from `service_client.c`, lines 41-44):**\n- `SC_PALETTE_SERVICE_URL` - Palette service base URL\n- `SC_TEXTURE_SERVICE_URL` - Texture service base URL\n- `SC_AUDIO_SERVICE_URL` - Audio service base URL\n- `SC_NARRATIVE_SERVICE_URL` - Narrative service base URL\n\n### 1.3 Backend Microservice Implementations\n\n| Service | Main Entry Point | Handler | Port |\n|---------|-----------------|---------|------|\n| **Texture Service** | `services/texture-service/src/main.c` | `services/texture-service/src/texture_handler.c` | 7002 |\n| **Palette Service** | `services/palette-service/src/main.c` | N/A (inline) | 7001 |\n| **Audio Service** | `services/audio-service/src/main.c` | TBD | 7003 |\n| **Narrative Service** | `services/narrative-service/src/main.c` | TBD | 7004 |\n\n**Current Backend HTTP Server Implementation:**\nAll microservices use **libmicrohttpd** for HTTP serving. From `texture-service/src/main.c` (lines 415-421):\n\n```c\nsvc.daemon = MHD_start_daemon(MHD_USE_AUTO | MHD_USE_INTERNAL_POLLING_THREAD,\n                              svc.cfg.port,\n                              NULL, NULL,\n                              request_router, &svc,\n                              MHD_OPTION_CONNECTION_TIMEOUT, (unsigned int)10,\n                              MHD_OPTION_END);\n```\n\n### 1.4 Common Libraries\n\n| Library | Path | Purpose |\n|---------|------|---------|\n| **sc_common** | `libs/sc_common/` | Shared configuration, logging, error handling |\n| **sc_config.h** | `libs/sc_common/include/sc_config.h` | Runtime configuration structures |\n| **sc_logging.h** | `libs/sc_common/include/sc_logging.h` | Structured logging facade |\n| **sc_errors.h** | `libs/sc_common/include/sc_errors.h` | Error code definitions |\n\n### 1.5 Build System Files\n\n| Component | Path | Modifications Required |\n|-----------|------|----------------------|\n| **Root CMake** | `CMakeLists.txt` | Add gRPC/Protobuf dependencies |\n| **Gateway CMake** | `api-gateway/CMakeLists.txt` | Link gRPC libraries, add proto compilation |\n| **Texture Service CMake** | `services/texture-service/CMakeLists.txt` | Add gRPC server support |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Data Flow Analysis\n\n### 2.1 Current Request Flow (Based on `data_flow.puml`)\n\nThe PlantUML diagram (`docs/architecture/data_flow.puml`) illustrates the following synchronous request path:\n\n```\nClient \u2192 API Gateway \u2192 Rate Limiter \u2192 Redis Cache \u2192 Request Validator \u2192 GraphQL Resolver\n                                                                              \u2193\n                                                                    [Texture Service]\n                                                                              \u2193\n                                                                    PostgreSQL/Redis\n                                                                              \u2193\n                                                                    Response \u2190 Client\n```\n\n### 2.2 Detailed Request Flow: API Gateway to Texture Service\n\n#### Step 1: Client Request Arrival\n**File:** `api-gateway/src/gateway_server.c` (lines 390-468)\n\n```c\nstatic int access_handler_cb(void *cls, struct MHD_Connection *conn,\n                             const char *url, const char *method, ...)\n```\n\n1. Request received by libmicrohttpd\n2. Rate limiting check via token bucket (`rate_limit_get_bucket()`)\n3. URL routing to appropriate handler\n\n#### Step 2: GraphQL Resolution\n**File:** `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c` (lines 184-210)\n\n```c\nstatic json_t *resolve_palette(const json_t *args, void *user_data, GQLError **gql_err)\n{\n    // Extract arguments\n    const char *id = json_string_value(json_object_get(args, \"id\"));\n\n    // Rate limit check\n    if (rate_limiter_acquire(ctx->limiter) != 0) { ... }\n\n    // Build upstream URL\n    char url[512];\n    snprintf(url, sizeof(url), \"%s/palettes/%s\", PALETTE_SERVICE_BASE_URL, id);\n\n    // Call upstream service via HTTP\n    json_t *payload = http_json_get(url, ctx->log, gql_err);\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 3: Service Client Call\n**File:** `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` (lines 247-330)\n\n```c\nstatic int perform_request(sc_service_client_t *client, const char *url,\n                           const char *method, const char *json_body,\n                           long *http_status, cJSON **out_body)\n{\n    // Uses libcurl for HTTP communication\n    curl_easy_setopt(h, CURLOPT_URL, url);\n    curl_easy_setopt(h, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, hdrs);\n    res = curl_easy_perform(h);\n}\n```\n\n**Key Data Structures:**\n- `sc_service_client_t` - Client state with per-service URLs, metrics\n- `response_buf_t` - Dynamic response buffer\n- Request/response serialization via **cJSON**\n\n#### Step 4: Texture Service Processing\n**File:** `services/texture-service/src/main.c` (lines 347-378)\n\n```c\nstatic enum MHD_Result request_router(void *cls, struct MHD_Connection *connection,\n                                      const char *url, const char *method, ...)\n{\n    if (strcmp(url, \"/healthz\") == 0) {\n        return handle_healthz(connection);\n    }\n    else if (strcmp(url, \"/v1/noise\") == 0) {\n        return handle_noise(svc, connection);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Handler Processing:**\n**File:** `services/texture-service/src/texture_handler.c` (lines 132-194)\n\n```c\nTexture *texture_handler_create(TextureHandler *handler, const TextureInput *input,\n                                TextureError *err)\n{\n    // Validation\n    if (!_validate_texture_input(input, err)) return NULL;\n\n    // Build domain object\n    tx.id = _generate_uuid();\n\n    // Repository persistence\n    bool persist_ok = repository_save_texture(state->repo, &tx, err);\n\n    // Metrics update\n    if (state->metrics) metrics_counter_inc(state->metrics, \"texture_created_total\", 1);\n\n    return texture_clone(&tx, err);\n}\n```\n\n#### Step 5: Response Path\n\n1. Handler returns JSON response via `MHD_create_response_from_buffer()`\n2. Response flows back through libmicrohttpd\n3. Gateway receives HTTP response via libcurl\n4. Gateway parses JSON via `cJSON_Parse()`\n5. GraphQL resolver returns payload to client\n\n---\n\n## 3. Migration Strategy Proposal\n\n### 3.1 Overview: Phased Migration Approach\n\nThe migration will follow a **strangler fig pattern** with parallel systems operating simultaneously. This ensures zero downtime and allows for gradual rollout with easy rollback capability.\n\n```\nPhase 1: Infrastructure Setup (gRPC dependencies, proto definitions)\n    \u2193\nPhase 2: Texture Service Dual-Protocol Support (gRPC + HTTP)\n    \u2193\nPhase 3: API Gateway gRPC Client Integration (Feature Flag)\n    \u2193\nPhase 4: Traffic Migration (Gradual rollout)\n    \u2193\nPhase 5: Legacy HTTP Deprecation & Removal\n```\n\n### 3.2 Phase 1: Infrastructure Setup\n\n#### 3.2.1 Protocol Buffer Definition\n\n**New File:** `protos/texture.proto`\n\n```protobuf\nsyntax = \"proto3\";\n\npackage synestheticcanvas.texture.v1;\n\noption c_enable_arenas = true;\n\nservice TextureService {\n    rpc CreateTexture(CreateTextureRequest) returns (CreateTextureResponse);\n    rpc GetTexture(GetTextureRequest) returns (GetTextureResponse);\n    rpc ListTextures(ListTexturesRequest) returns (ListTexturesResponse);\n    rpc DeleteTexture(DeleteTextureRequest) returns (DeleteTextureResponse);\n    rpc GetTextureRaw(GetTextureRawRequest) returns (stream TextureChunk);\n}\n\nmessage CreateTextureRequest {\n    string name = 1;\n    string color_profile = 2;\n    uint32 width = 3;\n    uint32 height = 4;\n    float frequency = 5;\n}\n\nmessage CreateTextureResponse {\n    string id = 1;\n    uint32 width = 2;\n    uint32 height = 3;\n    string created_at = 4;\n}\n\nmessage GetTextureRequest {\n    string id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage GetTextureResponse {\n    string id = 1;\n    string name = 2;\n    string color_profile = 3;\n    uint32 width = 4;\n    uint32 height = 5;\n    string created_at = 6;\n}\n\nmessage ListTexturesRequest {\n    uint32 page_size = 1;\n    string page_token = 2;\n}\n\nmessage ListTexturesResponse {\n    repeated GetTextureResponse textures = 1;\n    string next_page_token = 2;\n    uint32 total_count = 3;\n}\n\nmessage DeleteTextureRequest {\n    string id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage DeleteTextureResponse {\n    bool success = 1;\n}\n\nmessage GetTextureRawRequest {\n    string id = 1;\n}\n\nmessage TextureChunk {\n    bytes data = 1;\n    uint64 offset = 2;\n    uint64 total_size = 3;\n}\n```\n\n#### 3.2.2 Root CMakeLists.txt Modifications\n\n**File:** `CMakeLists.txt` (Add after line 127)\n\n```cmake\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#  gRPC and Protocol Buffers Support\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\noption(SC_ENABLE_GRPC \"Enable gRPC support for inter-service communication\" OFF)\n\nif(SC_ENABLE_GRPC)\n    find_package(Protobuf REQUIRED)\n    find_package(gRPC REQUIRED)\n\n    # Locate grpc_cpp_plugin for code generation\n    find_program(GRPC_CPP_PLUGIN grpc_cpp_plugin REQUIRED)\n\n    # Proto compilation function\n    function(add_proto_library TARGET_NAME PROTO_FILE)\n        get_filename_component(PROTO_PATH ${PROTO_FILE} DIRECTORY)\n        get_filename_component(PROTO_NAME ${PROTO_FILE} NAME_WE)\n\n        set(PROTO_SRCS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.pb.c\")\n        set(PROTO_HDRS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.pb.h\")\n        set(GRPC_SRCS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.grpc.pb.c\")\n        set(GRPC_HDRS \"${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}/${PROTO_NAME}.grpc.pb.h\")\n\n        add_custom_command(\n            OUTPUT ${PROTO_SRCS} ${PROTO_HDRS} ${GRPC_SRCS} ${GRPC_HDRS}\n            COMMAND protobuf::protoc\n            ARGS --proto_path=${PROTO_PATH}\n                 --c_out=${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}\n                 --grpc_out=${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR}\n                 --plugin=protoc-gen-grpc=${GRPC_CPP_PLUGIN}\n                 ${PROTO_FILE}\n            DEPENDS ${PROTO_FILE}\n        )\n\n        add_library(${TARGET_NAME} STATIC ${PROTO_SRCS} ${GRPC_SRCS})\n        target_include_directories(${TARGET_NAME} PUBLIC ${CMAKE_CURRENT_BINARY_DIR})\n        target_link_libraries(${TARGET_NAME} PUBLIC protobuf::libprotobuf-c gRPC::grpc)\n    endfunction()\n\n    # Compile proto files\n    add_proto_library(texture_proto ${PROJECT_SOURCE_DIR}/protos/texture.proto)\nendif()\n```\n\n### 3.3 Phase 2: Texture Service Dual-Protocol Support\n\nThe texture service will be modified to listen on **two ports simultaneously**: one for the existing HTTP/REST API and one for gRPC.\n\n#### 3.3.1 Texture Service CMakeLists.txt Modifications\n\n**File:** `services/texture-service/CMakeLists.txt` (Add after line 157)\n\n```cmake\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#  gRPC Server Support (Optional)\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\noption(TEXTURESVC_ENABLE_GRPC \"Enable gRPC server endpoint\" OFF)\n\nif(TEXTURESVC_ENABLE_GRPC)\n    if(NOT TARGET texture_proto)\n        message(FATAL_ERROR \"texture_proto target not found. Build with -DSC_ENABLE_GRPC=ON\")\n    endif()\n\n    target_sources(texture_service PRIVATE\n        src/grpc_server.c\n        src/grpc_handlers.c\n    )\n\n    target_link_libraries(texture_service\n        PRIVATE\n            texture_proto\n            gRPC::grpc\n            gRPC::grpc++\n    )\n\n    target_compile_definitions(texture_service PRIVATE ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER=1)\nendif()\n```\n\n#### 3.3.2 Dual-Protocol Main Entry Point\n\n**New File:** `services/texture-service/src/grpc_server.c`\n\n```c\n/**\n * gRPC Server implementation for Texture Service\n * Runs alongside HTTP server for parallel protocol support\n */\n\n#include <grpc/grpc.h>\n#include <grpc/support/log.h>\n#include \"texture.grpc.pb-c.h\"\n#include \"texture_handler.h\"\n\n#define GRPC_DEFAULT_PORT 17002  // gRPC on separate port\n\ntypedef struct {\n    grpc_server *server;\n    grpc_completion_queue *cq;\n    TextureHandler *handler;\n    volatile bool running;\n} grpc_texture_server_t;\n\n// gRPC service method implementations\nstatic void handle_create_texture(grpc_texture_server_t *srv,\n                                  const CreateTextureRequest *req,\n                                  CreateTextureResponse *resp) {\n    TextureInput input = {\n        .name = req->name,\n        .color_profile = req->color_profile,\n        .width = req->width,\n        .height = req->height\n    };\n\n    TextureError err = {0};\n    Texture *tx = texture_handler_create(srv->handler, &input, &err);\n\n    if (tx) {\n        resp->id = strdup(tx->id);\n        resp->width = tx->width;\n        resp->height = tx->height;\n        // Format timestamp\n        char ts[32];\n        strftime(ts, sizeof(ts), \"%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ\", gmtime(&tx->created_at));\n        resp->created_at = strdup(ts);\n        texture_free(tx);\n    }\n}\n\ngrpc_texture_server_t *grpc_texture_server_create(TextureHandler *handler, uint16_t port);\nvoid grpc_texture_server_serve(grpc_texture_server_t *srv);\nvoid grpc_texture_server_stop(grpc_texture_server_t *srv);\nvoid grpc_texture_server_destroy(grpc_texture_server_t *srv);\n```\n\n#### 3.3.3 Modified main.c for Dual-Protocol\n\n**File:** `services/texture-service/src/main.c` (Modifications)\n\n```c\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER\n#include \"grpc_server.h\"\n#include <pthread.h>\n\nstatic pthread_t g_grpc_thread;\nstatic grpc_texture_server_t *g_grpc_server = NULL;\n\nstatic void *grpc_server_thread(void *arg) {\n    grpc_texture_server_t *srv = (grpc_texture_server_t *)arg;\n    grpc_texture_server_serve(srv);\n    return NULL;\n}\n#endif\n\nint main(void)\n{\n    ServiceCtx svc;\n    config_set_defaults(&svc.cfg);\n\n    // ... existing HTTP setup ...\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER\n    // Start gRPC server on separate port\n    uint16_t grpc_port = (uint16_t)sc_u16_from_env(\"TEXTURE_GRPC_PORT\", 17002);\n    g_grpc_server = grpc_texture_server_create(svc.handler, grpc_port);\n    if (g_grpc_server) {\n        pthread_create(&g_grpc_thread, NULL, grpc_server_thread, g_grpc_server);\n        log_msg(LOG_INFO, \"gRPC server started on port %u\", grpc_port);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    // Start HTTP daemon (existing code)\n    svc.daemon = MHD_start_daemon(...);\n\n    while (!g_shutdown)\n        sleep(1);\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_SERVER\n    if (g_grpc_server) {\n        grpc_texture_server_stop(g_grpc_server);\n        pthread_join(g_grpc_thread, NULL);\n        grpc_texture_server_destroy(g_grpc_server);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    MHD_stop_daemon(svc.daemon);\n    return EXIT_SUCCESS;\n}\n```\n\n### 3.4 Phase 3: API Gateway gRPC Client Integration\n\n#### 3.4.1 Gateway CMakeLists.txt Modifications\n\n**File:** `api-gateway/CMakeLists.txt` (Add after line 147)\n\n```cmake\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#  gRPC Client Support\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\noption(GATEWAY_ENABLE_GRPC \"Enable gRPC client for upstream services\" OFF)\n\nif(GATEWAY_ENABLE_GRPC)\n    if(NOT TARGET texture_proto)\n        message(FATAL_ERROR \"texture_proto target not found. Build with -DSC_ENABLE_GRPC=ON\")\n    endif()\n\n    target_sources(api_gateway PRIVATE\n        src/services/grpc_client.c\n    )\n\n    target_link_libraries(api_gateway\n        PRIVATE\n            texture_proto\n            gRPC::grpc\n    )\n\n    target_compile_definitions(api_gateway PRIVATE ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT=1)\nendif()\n```\n\n#### 3.4.2 Feature Flag for Protocol Selection\n\n**File:** `api-gateway/src/services/service_client.c` (Modifications)\n\n```c\n// Add to sc_service_client_t structure\nstruct sc_service_client\n{\n    // ... existing fields ...\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT\n    /* gRPC channels */\n    grpc_channel *texture_grpc_channel;\n    bool use_grpc_texture;  // Feature flag\n#endif\n};\n\n// Modified initialization\nsc_service_client_t *sc_service_client_new(void)\n{\n    // ... existing code ...\n\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT\n    // Check feature flag\n    cli->use_grpc_texture = sc_bool_from_env(\"SC_USE_GRPC_TEXTURE\", false);\n\n    if (cli->use_grpc_texture) {\n        const char *grpc_addr = getenv(\"SC_TEXTURE_GRPC_URL\") ?: \"texture-service:17002\";\n        cli->texture_grpc_channel = grpc_insecure_channel_create(grpc_addr, NULL, NULL);\n        LOG_INF(\"gRPC enabled for texture service: %s\", grpc_addr);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    return cli;\n}\n\n// Modified call function\nint sc_service_client_call(sc_service_client_t *cli,\n                           sc_service_endp_t    endpoint,\n                           const char          *method,\n                           const char          *path,\n                           const char          *request_json,\n                           cJSON              **response_json,\n                           long                *http_status)\n{\n#ifdef ENABLE_GRPC_CLIENT\n    if (endpoint == SC_EP_TEXTURE && cli->use_grpc_texture) {\n        return sc_service_client_call_grpc(cli, path, request_json,\n                                           response_json, http_status);\n    }\n#endif\n\n    // Fall back to HTTP\n    return sc_service_client_call_http(cli, endpoint, method, path,\n                                       request_json, response_json, http_status);\n}\n```\n\n### 3.5 Phase 4: Traffic Migration Strategy\n\n#### 3.5.1 Deployment Configuration\n\n**Modified docker-compose.yml:**\n\n```yaml\ntexture_service:\n  environment:\n    <<: *default-env\n    SERVICE_PORT: 7002\n    TEXTURE_GRPC_PORT: 17002  # New gRPC port\n  ports:\n    - \"7002:7002\"    # HTTP (existing)\n    - \"17002:17002\"  # gRPC (new)\n\napi_gateway:\n  environment:\n    <<: *default-env\n    SC_USE_GRPC_TEXTURE: \"false\"  # Start with HTTP\n    SC_TEXTURE_GRPC_URL: \"texture_service:17002\"\n```\n\n#### 3.5.2 Gradual Rollout Process\n\n1. **Week 1:** Deploy texture service with dual-protocol support\n   - Monitor gRPC health endpoint\n   - Verify no performance degradation\n\n2. **Week 2:** Enable gRPC for internal testing\n   ```bash\n   export SC_USE_GRPC_TEXTURE=true  # On test gateway instances\n   ```\n\n3. **Week 3:** Canary deployment (5% traffic)\n   - Use load balancer weighted routing\n   - Monitor error rates and latency\n\n4. **Week 4:** Gradual increase (25% \u2192 50% \u2192 100%)\n\n5. **Week 5:** Deprecate HTTP endpoints (keep for rollback)\n\n### 3.6 Phase 5: Legacy HTTP Deprecation\n\nAfter successful migration:\n\n1. Remove HTTP endpoints from texture service\n2. Remove HTTP client code from gateway\n3. Update CMakeLists.txt to make gRPC the default\n4. Remove feature flags\n\n---\n\n## 4. Risk Assessment\n\n### 4.1 Risk 1: Build System Complexity\n\n**Severity:** HIGH\n**Likelihood:** HIGH\n\n**Description:**\nAdding gRPC to a pure C project introduces significant build system complexity. gRPC's C implementation requires:\n- Protocol Buffers compiler and runtime (`protobuf-c`)\n- gRPC C core library (`grpc`)\n- C++ toolchain (gRPC core has C++ dependencies)\n\n**Evidence:**\nCurrent CMakeLists.txt uses pure C with `-std=c17` standard (see `api-gateway/CMakeLists.txt`, line 66). gRPC-C requires linking against C++ runtime.\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Use `grpc` C-core library instead of `grpc++`\n- Consider using `protobuf-c` for pure C protobuf support\n- Provide comprehensive Docker build images with pre-installed dependencies\n- Implement FetchContent fallbacks for missing system packages\n\n### 4.2 Risk 2: Performance Regression\n\n**Severity:** MEDIUM\n**Likelihood:** MEDIUM\n\n**Description:**\nThe current custom IPC uses UNIX domain sockets with minimal framing overhead (4-byte length prefix). gRPC introduces HTTP/2 framing overhead, protobuf serialization, and TLS handshakes (if enabled).\n\n**Evidence:**\nFrom `libs/sc_ipc/src/sc_ipc.c` (line 315-340), the current protocol uses simple `writev()` syscalls with minimal overhead.\n\n**Performance Characteristics Comparison:**\n\n| Aspect | Custom IPC | gRPC (HTTP/2) |\n|--------|-----------|---------------|\n| Framing overhead | 4 bytes | ~20-50 bytes |\n| Serialization | JSON/raw | Protobuf (binary) |\n| Connection setup | None (UNIX socket) | TCP + HTTP/2 handshake |\n| Latency (typical) | <1ms | 1-5ms |\n| Throughput | Higher | Lower (due to framing) |\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Enable gRPC keep-alive to reduce connection overhead\n- Use streaming for large payloads (texture data)\n- Consider Unix Domain Socket transport for gRPC (if same host)\n- Benchmark before and after migration\n\n### 4.3 Risk 3: Operational Complexity During Transition\n\n**Severity:** MEDIUM\n**Likelihood:** HIGH\n\n**Description:**\nRunning a hybrid system with both HTTP and gRPC endpoints increases operational burden:\n- Doubled port exposure and monitoring\n- Complex debugging (two protocols)\n- Inconsistent behavior during transition\n\n**Evidence:**\nDocker-compose configuration shows services already expose multiple ports (see `docker-compose.yml`, lines 59-61).\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Unified observability (OpenTelemetry supports both HTTP and gRPC)\n- Single health check endpoint covering both protocols\n- Clear runbooks for protocol-specific troubleshooting\n- Automated testing for both code paths\n\n### 4.4 Risk 4: Serialization Compatibility\n\n**Severity:** MEDIUM\n**Likelihood:** LOW\n\n**Description:**\nThe current system uses JSON for all payloads. Migration to Protobuf requires careful schema definition to maintain backward compatibility.\n\n**Evidence:**\nFrom `api-gateway/graphql/resolvers.c` (line 125), responses are parsed with `json_loads()`. From `services/texture-service/src/texture_handler.c` (line 373-394), JSON serialization is used throughout.\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Define protobuf schemas that map 1:1 with existing JSON\n- Add `json_name` options for field name compatibility\n- Maintain JSON gateway for external consumers\n- Version protobuf schemas from the start\n\n### 4.5 Risk 5: Debugging and Observability\n\n**Severity:** LOW\n**Likelihood:** MEDIUM\n\n**Description:**\nJSON payloads are human-readable and easy to debug. Protobuf binary encoding requires additional tooling.\n\n**Evidence:**\nCurrent logging in `service_client.c` (lines 337-354) outputs JSON directly to stderr.\n\n**Mitigation:**\n- Use gRPC reflection service for introspection\n- Implement protobuf-to-JSON logging adapter\n- Use `grpcurl` or similar tools for debugging\n- Enable gRPC verbose logging during development\n\n---\n\n## 5. New gRPC-Based Communication Flow\n\n### 5.1 Request Flow Diagram\n\n```\n Maintain HTTP fallback for rollback capability\n\n**Timeline Estimate:**\n- Phase 1 (Infrastructure): 2-3 weeks\n- Phase 2 (Texture Service): 2-3 weeks\n- Phase 3 (Gateway Client): 2 weeks\n- Phase 4 (Migration): 4-6 weeks\n- Phase 5 (Cleanup): 1-2 weeks\n\n**Total:** 11-16 weeks for complete migration\n\n---\n\n## 7. # Technical Report: Migration from Custom IPC to gRPC

## SynestheticCanvas API Suite - Inter-Service Communication Migration Analysis

**Author:** Principal Engineer
**Date:** 2026-02-02
**Version:** 1.0

---

## Executive Summary

This report provides a comprehensive technical analysis of migrating the SynestheticCanvas API Suite from its current custom Inter-Process Communication (IPC) library (`sc_ipc`) to gRPC. The analysis covers component identification, data flow analysis, a phased migration strategy, and risk assessment. The migration is deemed feasible with careful planning, particularly around build system modifications and a parallel deployment strategy to ensure zero-downtime transitions.

---

## 1. Component Identification: Current IPC System

### 1.1 Shared IPC Library (`sc_ipc`)

The core inter-service communication is built on a custom UNIX domain socket-based IPC library.

| Component | Path | Description |
|-----------|------|-------------|
| **Header** | `libs/sc_ipc/include/sc_ipc.h` | Public API definitions, error codes, message types |
| **Implementation** | `libs/sc_ipc/src/sc_ipc.c` | Socket management, message framing, send/recv operations |

**Key API Functions (from `sc_ipc.h`):**

```c
// Server-side initialization
int sc_ipc_server_init(sc_ipc_channel_t *srv, const char *endpoint, size_t backlog);
int sc_ipc_accept(const sc_ipc_channel_t *srv, sc_ipc_channel_t *out_cli, uint32_t timeout_ms);

// Client-side initialization
int sc_ipc_client_init(sc_ipc_channel_t *cli, const char *endpoint, uint32_t timeout_ms);

// Message I/O
int sc_ipc_send_msg(sc_ipc_channel_t *chan, sc_ipc_msg_type_t type, const void *payload,
                    size_t payload_len, uint64_t correlation_id, uint32_t timeout_ms);
int sc_ipc_recv_msg(sc_ipc_channel_t *cha
... (truncated)
